<!-- POST START: id=12055563 num=293 author=Fellowed author_id=306053 date=2014-01-03T19:36:07+0000 -->
### Post #293

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12055563 |
| Author | Fellowed |
| Author ID | 306053 |
| Date | Jan 3, 2014 at 7:36 PM |
| Page | 15 |

Found this to be a mixed but overall good experience. Personally I was more interested in AL-LAD but that doesn't seem to be around anymore (sadly) so got these instead. Myself and 2 others took one tab each. The effects were very similar to acid but seemed to change more rapidly. It's difficult to explain but it was like each effect came on in different stages and never stayed consistent for very long. One minute I'd have the typical LSD body feeling but few visuals, then the next no body feeling and tripping intensely. At one point we all got the giggles but one moment we were laughing, then the next almost trying not to. Very confusing! Also, it never felt like we were all on the same "level" as these changing effects weren't happening to us in unison which made it a less social experience than I usually find when I have LSD. In fact I found that I most enjoyed the experience when I was by myself at which point the rapid changes in mood didn't seem to matter. The solution to this strangeness seemed to be watching programs (lots of cartoons) as it gave us all a mutual audio/visual point of reference.

<!-- POST END: id=12055563 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12058166 num=300 author=Contained author_id=220823 date=2014-01-05T00:14:07+0000 -->
### Post #300

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12058166 |

| Author ID | 220823 |

| Page | 15 |

Mixed one tab (150ug) of lsz with 60mg pure mdma (30mg up the nose, 30mg orally) and continuous little bumps of ketamine last night while in a cabin in the forest. I've never been so comfortable in my life. I kind of lost track of time so I don't know if I'll be able to write a legitimate trip report but I'll try.


One of the most interesting points of the trip I was laying on a big hammock with 3 other friends covered in a pile of blankets and pillows looking up at the stars, all of the sudden it felt like the very center of my forehead opened up and I could feel and visualize this ray of energy seeping into the "opened" hole in my head. It really was an indescribable feeling but the only thing I can equate it to is the feeling of being recharged. This lasted for maybe 20 minutes of clock time but in the moment it's hard to say how long it felt.  All of the sudden the feeling started to spread through my whole body and I couldn't really tell where my skin ended. It was a journey.

<!-- POST END: id=12058166 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12058513 num=301 author=Una author_id=230967 date=2014-01-05T02:49:22+0000 -->
### Post #301

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12058513 |
| Author | Una |
| Author ID | 230967 |
| Date | Jan 5, 2014 at 2:49 AM |
| Page | 16 |

I did 300ug of LSZ and for all intents and purposes found it to be indistinguishable from LSD. Granted I have not had a proper trip with LSD in a couple years, but if some one sold me that as LSD I do not think I could tell the difference.


I think that dose was perfect for me. Would probably recommend 150ug to green trippers, to be safe.


There was a group of four of us, and during the peak it started to get to the point where we were having trouble functioning and communicating in any kind of productive way. But just when you started to think: "Oh man, I think I took too much, this is getting hard to control," it started to subside in intensity after a peak of about 4 hours or so. There was a lot of spontaneous laughter, you know, when you burst out laughing just because some one else is laughing, to the point where your eyes are watering and your sides hurt from laughing so much. And still you keep laughing.


There was no abnormal body load like I have seen some people mention. No nausea. Just a general tenseness in the muscles. Much like I get with LSD.


I would say the timeline went something like this: 


Dropped at 10:30pm. Tripped pretty hard from 11:30pm till 2:30am. The intensity started to ebb after 2:30am, but with a steady plateau till 5:00am. Was still pretty fucked at at 7:00am, but would not call it tripping per se. At around noon the next day almost all the visuals were gone and felt pretty much at baseline, but "tweaked"


Could not fall asleep until around 10pm the next day though.


BRILLIANT closed eye visuals ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=12058513 -->

Did 300 mcg of LSZ recently. Very similar to LSD, almost indistinguishable, and maybe even more - to AL-LAD. 

More side effects on come-up then both, though, something with ears and swallowing. Come-up took 1.5 hours, first effects after 40 mins.

300mcg was very light trip for me, but I have extremely low sensitivity to all psychs.

I think this is great substance, feelings of wonder, party, happiness, afterglow in next days.

But I think I like  AL-LAD even more.

Get it while it is still legal in most places.

Also, orgasm on LSZ is something very wonderful. It's like colored shards of happiness everywhere,  you just smile, and you are feeling great.

<!-- POST START: id=12078062 num=307 author=P Schwangles author_id=293063 date=2014-01-13T23:23:52+0000 -->
### Post #307

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12078062 |
| Author | P Schwangles |
| Author ID | 293063 |
| Date | Jan 13, 2014 at 11:23 PM |
| Page | 16 |

In response to the question of the "lysergic feel", I found both 150mcg of Al LAD and LSZ to have very obvious lysergic similarities to LSD.  By comparison, they do not feel like a phenethylamine or tryptamine.  In fact, I would say that only Al LAD had noticeable differences at this dosage - similar feel, but clearly distinct, and it seems that the distinctions are a little different from person to person (The one time I tried it, I found it to be less kaleidoscopic and visual, but also to be kinda easy-going and pleasant, despite the sharper/shorter peak).  

One night about a month ago, I tried 150mcg of LSZ and my fiancee (less inclined to try new things until I've tested the waters) ate 100mcg LSD, and we were pretty much in the exact same zone.  If someone had told me I'd eaten 100mcg hit of LSD, I would have believed them, and I've eaten LSD hundreds of times.  As someone else mentioned, the only benefit of LSZ over LSD is the legality, and perhaps the dosage regularity.  Maybe they become more distinct at a higher dosage, but at the standard "one hit" level, 150 mcg LSZ and 100 mcg LSD were very very similar to me.

<!-- POST END: id=12078062 -->

This is all very interesting. I found an apparently extremely reliable site selling LSZ and AL-LAD but unfortunately, while prices are decent, they are in Euros, with the (again) dwindling Canadian dollar I'd get screwed buying some of these pre-laid blotter. And I still can get LSD sheets whenever I want for about the same prices, well whenever I want, it is easy as hell to get the same old print circulating in Canada since a decade+ (multiple logos of punk rock bands, cartoon characters, tim leary, sid vicious and other funny/weird drawings per blotter) that come in either red on white, blue on white and green on white 1/4 inch x 1/4 inch hits. They are very good when obtained at the "i only sell sheets buddy" level, but when some random punk / skater and now from the identity-less younger generation, they will be degraded by poor manipulation, storage etc.


I think this print is made in Quebec only but the actual LSD comes from BC. Which is why we are flooded by those hits during the winter, and when everyone feels like tripping (summer), it starts becoming extremely scarce. At least this same cycle happened from the early 2000's to around 2008 when I last did those  hits.


Anyways...those LSD and AL-LAD providers could be original...I have never seen windowpane/geltab hits in my life and only saw orange Microdots in 1999 when the local market was flooded with orange dots with LSD and red Nexus (2c-B) pills. I only had 2c-b then cos I knew it didn't last long so I never had a microdot cos I was still pretty scared of drugs back then.


In retrospect I should have stayed. This one random hit I took that didn't have the so ever present design of blotter print sometimes in late 2002 (they were playing card symbols hits...quite the gamble indeed), was a DOB hit, was fun for maybe 5-6 hours, the remaing 20 to 22 hours were just anxiety and hell. I know they were DOB, because they certainly weren't DOM, and other DOx weren't sold online then still. But lots of reports on the internet from police seizures trying to cause hysteria (kinda warranted, as it was sold as "acid" but wasn't) were appearing in the media in those days reporting DOB blotters in Canada and Australia in particular. This DOB hit hurt me mentally for 3 years certainly, causing a lot of psychosomatic "pain" and now i'm just another guy on suboxone...with actual pain issues that are really undertreated by the crappy painkiller suboxone is. But this isn't the drug biography thread so I'll stop now. The etaqualone and valium are making me want to talk and talk and talk ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

> 			Skinner wasn't happy with Pickard's LSZ? I've never read that. do you have a source by chance?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — osla4n said:


The Rolling Stones article + testimony from Neurocunt girl. The Rolling Stones article is huge and old but still easy to find online. I think someone pasted it in a post over at the shroomery.


Here's what Neurorape Girl said in her Vice interview (from another site, it is verbatim) :


[http://countyourculture.com/2011/12/01/non-lsd-ergoloids/](http://countyourculture.com/2011/12/01/non-lsd-ergoloids/)


    There were other novel substances as well. Leonard [Pickard] made a new LSD analog called “diazedine,” though I don’t know exactly what that was either.


    Are you familiar with lysergic acid 2,4-dimethylazetidide?*


    No, but they were calling this diazedine. It was also crazy, but nothing earth-shattering. Leonard [Pickard] gave it to Todd [Skinner] in a bottle of Everclear for testing, and we would dose a capful at a time. Apparently, diazedine failed to be doable on a large scale because the production costs were too high and the yields too low. Diazedine caused a lot of stress between Todd and Leonard, because they had high expectations for it as an LSD alternative.


    *Lysergic acid 2,4-dimethylazetidide (aka LSZ) belongs to a very small group of serotonergic psychedelics that surpass LSD in potency. Aside from the fact that “diazedine” is a lexical clipping of dimethylazetidine (diazedine<dimethylazetidine), the first paper describing the chemistry and pharmacology of LSZ came out of a laboratory at Purdue University, where Leonard had previously studied under the renowned chemist David Nichols. Though the paper was published after Leonard’s arrest, it is still quite likely he was aware of the preliminary research. When I asked Dr. Nichols whether he thought Pickard may have produced LSZ, he replied, “Leonard knew of our work, of that I am certain.” Rumors of LSZ distributed on blotter paper (purportedly under the name λ) have circulated for years, though there are few confirmed reports of its existence. Of course, the name diazedine is ambiguous and could be referring to just about anything, but I would bet a kilo of benzotriazole-1-yl-oxy-tris-pyrrolidino-phosphonium hexafluorophosphate that LSZ and diazedine are one and the same.


    From an interview of Krystal Cole, Life is a Cosmic Giggle on the Breath of the Universe, Vice Magazine.

<!-- POST START: id=12182193 num=331 author=FunctionalOlfactio author_id=293108 date=2014-03-02T14:57:27+0000 -->
### Post #331

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12182193 |
| Author | FunctionalOlfactio |
| Author ID | 293108 |
| Date | Mar 2, 2014 at 2:57 PM |
| Page | 17 |

The isomers each appear to display very different binding properties. Discrimination studies showed the SS isomer to be most potent in animal models. This doesn't guarantee similar effects in humans. The ratio of 5ht1a and 5ht2a appears to change the subjective character of psychedelics in humans. The ratio in LSD is ~ 1 to 3 (1) and in SS-LSZ ~ 1 to 16 (1). SS-LSZ appears to show significant selectivity for 5ht1a over 5ht2a as compared to LSD.


I don't have direct experience with any LSZ isomer. My concern based on the data and experience is that the effects might greatly differ from LSD. Someone inexperienced might misinterpret the information available on LSZ, manage to obtain isometrically pure SS-LSZ , and distribute the chemical. The SS-LSZ would field test as LSD and could cause destructive consequences to the people who unwittingly consume the chemical thinking they received LSD.


The overall effects of psychedelics are dependent upon many variables. The only true test would be a human assessment. SS-LSZ might have very different effects than LSD. My goal is to emphasize the uncertainty and resultant risk with LSZ.


Reference:

1 [http://www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/pdf/azetidine-lsd.pdf](http://www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/pdf/azetidine-lsd.pdf)

[http://www.maps.org](http://www.maps.org)

| Post ID | 12186652 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 4, 2014 at 6:26 PM |
| Page | 17 |

Likely there is some.  All psychedelics are cross-tolerant to some degree.  However I would expect the cross-tolerance to not be too severe, as it would be, say, between AMT and MDMA (both releasers and entactogens).

<!-- POST END: id=12186652 -->

I swallowed a blotter tab of this whole yesterday, no chewing. I wish I had chewed it a bit first cause the blotter got stuck in my throat on the way down, took about 15 minutes of swallowing to get it to go all the way down, a bit uncomfortable ![:|](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/eyesclosed.gif)


I'd concur that LSZ is pretty damn close to LSD. I feel like it's slightly different, but I can't say how, and I think I'd have to do it a few more times before I'd be able to put my finger on what's different about it. I wouldn't be able to tell the difference in a blind test. Dropped 150ug at 4:30pm, by 2am was still a bit too wide awake to sleep, drifted off by about 2:30am, so it seems about a 10hr commitment for me. Woke up in the middle of the night feeling a little bit trippy still. Next day, feeling focused and afterglow effects. I like it.

<!-- POST END: id=12208046 -->

> Click to expand...
> — David the Chansey said:


It would indeed be lovely to have a legal  lysergamide that makes for good fuel for high-powered high-dose trips to the psych ward^W^W^W^W, but I fear that LSZ may not be It.


450ug was too much for me in terms of bodyload. I had a queasy feeling in just about every part of my body I cared to focus my attention on. I'm pretty sure I could have found something wrong with my toes had I wanted to. There was also nausea - to put it in scientific terms, I don't often find myself hunched over the toilet, dry heaving in the hope that I can expel the cause of my stomach upset, but that's exactly what I did that day, and the wicked LSZ wouldn't even let me have that small victory, opting instead to keep me in the "feeling sick" mode for a couple more hours. 


Add on top of that a headache and an overall feeling of muscle  stiffness in the entire body, and it's not something I'd care to go through again. Which is a shame, because LSZ is an intriguing drug.


For what it's worth, I felt fine on 300ug. It was in fact very nice.


I concur that AL-LAD is more benign, and might just be the one for adventures north of a milligram.


By the way - if you google a little bit, you may come across some high-dose LSZ reports, including a 1mg LSZ trip report, which did not go very well for the reporting fella. I'd paste the link here, except I'm not sure if linking to the infamous D.F. website is considered kosher on Bluelight. Just google for *"Next I threw up into the bin next to me, the world was now a spiraling coloured mess every time i opened my eyes."* :D

<!-- POST START: id=12221988 num=360 author=Qofdeath3000 author_id=315882 date=2014-03-21T14:53:19+0000 -->
### Post #360

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12221988 |
| Author | Qofdeath3000 |
| Author ID | 315882 |
| Date | Mar 21, 2014 at 2:53 PM |
| Page | 18 |

I took a 150mcg blotter of this the other day. I had taken a blotter of 25c nboh about 3 days before, but I had a few of these and I was very curious about tolerance, and about the drug in general.


To sum up a long and strange trip report, I either didn't experience any real cross tolerance, or lsz is some powerful stuff. It took about 2 hours to do anything really interesting, a bit sedating at first, but once it hit me, it was like my first lsd trip all over again. This stuff is like the creeper weed of LSD, you start thinking you just got a bunch of crap then suddenly, you're toast lol.


The sky grew closer to me, and took on a red/golden hue. Everything was beautiful. I was fully separated mentally from my body. I had an incredible body buzz going. Nearly lost my ego. It kept getting stronger over the course of the next 4 hours too. By the end of it minutes were passing by so slowly it was like I could shovel the entire backyard, workout, have a smoke, eat, and poop and 2 minutes would pass. Crazy shit. The peak was very very much like acid. No real negative effects to report other than a general sedated feeling that I generally dont get from acid. 10/10 will buy again. In quantity.

<!-- POST END: id=12221988 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12223598 num=363 author=ZFC author_id=294749 date=2014-03-22T07:39:34+0000 -->
### Post #363

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12223598 |
| Author | ZFC |
| Author ID | 294749 |
| Date | Mar 22, 2014 at 7:39 AM |
| Page | 19 |

Better late than never: I finally sampled a full 150 µg blotter that had been sitting in a drawer for months.


Previous commenters here weren't joking when they said there was no visuals. No morphing, no CEV. But an incredibly useful mindfuck.

I am very happy I managed to get myself to do what I actually had planned to do during the trip: read a fascinating a book on spacetime physics. Usually reading while tripping is problematic when the letters morph around before your eyes. Not a problem here!


It's all I did for hours and hours, and it brought me some incredible insights.


So yeah, I loved it. It was more mental and serious than AL-LAD, or even LSD. And my experiences with AL-LAD were a lot more visual and "less serious" (read: "more fun"!)

<!-- POST END: id=12223598 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=12226287 num=364 author=perpetualdawn author_id=307995 date=2014-03-23T18:27:33+0000 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12227595 num=365 author=ZFC author_id=294749 date=2014-03-24T10:48:25+0000 -->
### Post #365

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12227595 |
| Author | ZFC |
| Author ID | 294749 |
| Date | Mar 24, 2014 at 10:48 AM |
| Page | 19 |

Well reading per se was not at all impaired, neither was comprehension. But I did find myself reading a paragraph, and then hanging there *thinking about it* and all its fascinating implications for 20 minutes (I don't call that being distracted). So I wouldn't say I was reading faster, I was actually reading slower, but this is because of all the fascinating insights caused by the reading.

<!-- POST END: id=12227595 -->

apparently lsz can be visual!


i say this because my previous trial at the same dose (150ug) were all devoid of anything visual except a bit of wavy ness to things... and no CEVs at all.


not so when in combos. LSZ taken after 3h from dropping ~0,75 mg DOC made everything very visual indeed. neither chem on its own would have given me the amount of visuals i had. heck it was about the same level as allad in this regard... still a pretty nice chem to have around.


@JG if you want to experience the full spectrum and power of a chem you already know the answer to your question... meaning you have to wait a while to be sure you get 100% effects. otherwise you can go ahead and trip a bit im sure but you ll keep having the impression that perhaps it wouldve been better had you waited a bit longer ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

| Post ID | 12249342 |

| Page | 19 |

**Edit:** TL;DR is at the bottom


Well three, maybe four (it sure feels like two sets of two blotters inside the vacuum pack but I don't want to break the seal until I'm gonna drop it due to concerns of it breaking down faster than normal acid or AL-LAD, which the vendors seem to suggest on things like SOS) 150ug tabs made their way to me in the post today and I'll probably be dropping two of them mid afternoon on Friday. This thread seems to be rife with heavily mixed reports although some seem to be from people wanting the perfect psychedelic experience then being disappointed due to things like nausea or body load. I really hope I get at least something of a visual experience as the previous 'acid' I had were two purple microdots which seemed to cumulatively be only a threshold dose (probably due to me swallowing what was likely a NBOMe).

If they seem to be weak after +2h I'll probably up my dose to 375/450 and see where I get from there, though only if I'm in a position where I won't inadvertently wreak havoc on all around me or freak out uncontrollably.

I'll try and keep a notepad on hand so I can write up a blow-by-blow report for you guys since LSZ receives much less coverage than AL-LAD and the reports seem to be heavily conflicting.

Just for the record the blotters are in a silver vacuum sealed packet (labeled with the full molecular name, a picture of the molecule and it's CAS number) which is currently being stored in my freezer so the only time the molecule could have degraded is when it was in transit to me, which according to when I got an 'item shipped' email would have been two days, but the possibility of a fourth tab hints that they may have forgotten to send the letter (first class post always arrives next day in ~95% of cases), depending on how the vendors store their product before shipping I hope to be getting a minimally degraded sample.


If the experience turns out to be shit and I still have some Z left over, I'll order some AL-LAD this week and do a trip report on a dual 300mcg dose the following Friday. If the experience turns out well I'll be happy that a second legal ergoloid can be added to my arsenal, which seems to be the way to go since the acid scene has gotten a little too much "Make profit, fuck customers over, pass off cheaper, shittier chemicals as LSD" in any case I'll probably want to bring either Al or Lizzie with me to the Netherlands this summer, just in case I can't find good cid there.

Apologies if I'm rambling a bit, I tend to do that; expect many edits as well.


**TL;DR** - Got 3 (maybe four) 150ug blotters of LSZ in the post today, I'll drop a 300mcg dose mid afternoon on Friday and write up a comprehensive trip report, the LSZ is stored in a way to help slow degradation of the sample which should help give a more accurate report on Z's effects.

### Post #376

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12250456 |
| Author | bropiate |
| Author ID | 172215 |
| Date | Apr 3, 2014 at 3:57 PM |
| Page | 19 |

Would you prefer people write down their plans or flood bluelight with "I just took X is Y going to happen to me now" threads? Writing down one's plans allows others to make suggestions as to possible alterations to that plan, like the two people below you. Encouraging people to post their plans also helps people who are less experienced not have a terrible experience, or in cases of other more dangerous drugs; end up dead. I'd say that making plans and letting others know about them is a good harm reductionist strategy, you can't change things once you've already taken the drug, so giving a day or two's notice, especially when it's your very first time trying a new and novel drug should be promoted heavily.

<!-- POST START: id=12277441 num=378 author=al-laddin author_id=320273 date=2014-04-16T00:34:32+0100 -->
### Post #378

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12277441 |
| Author | al-laddin |
| Author ID | 320273 |
| Date | Apr 16, 2014 at 12:34 AM |
| Page | 19 |

Trip report 150 ug LSZ blotter (LSZ marked on one side, molecule print on reverse)


Experience level - Low to high doses of LSD. Low to moderate doses Mescaline. Low to high doses psilocybin. Minimal experience with RCs. Very sensitive to psychedelics. 100- 120 UG LSD is enough for ego dissolution but have dosed as high as 500-700 ug. Most I have taken of psilocybin was just over two grams extremely potent "penis envy" strain. Resulted in full blown mystical experience and several year long after glow. Basically I feel that I am sensitive to psychedelics because many of my peers require more to get to the same place as I.


T-00 One third blotter is placed in mouth and lightly chewed (I figured, if allegedly "more potent than LSD" I should have felt more than threshold effects @ 50ug and decided to test this theory whilst getting my feet wet so to speak ). My partner in Crime, "S" decided to start with the same method of administration at 75ug. The taste was slightly bitter, exactly how normal LSD blotter taste to me, slightly bitter and metallic.


T-15 Im sensitive to tryptamines and ergolines, in fact Im sensitive to any shift in body sensations brought on by compounds so at this point I definatly felt off baseline, a general stimulation and mood lift not unlike what one would feel from a few espressos.


T-30 I and S decide to walk to the liquor store and pick up some beers to drink throughout the evening. Definatly feeling effects now. Frame like vision, laughter and humor comes easier, lights off of the cars are more noticeable. When we arrive at the store, upon entering I notice the effect I get with most psychs; dark to light environment is difficult for my eyes to adjust to. I notice that my whole visual field has that familiar "electric" overlay. Everything has that glow to it. I thought to myself "wow, at 50ug this seems very promising". At this point S is unsure if he feels anything.


T-45 We are back at the house and we make a fire in the front yard. I feel as though the LSZ is leveling off, but decide to give it another 15 minutes before titrating up. S says "fuck it" and eats his other half, now at 150ug , expressing hes not feeling much. 


T-1:00 Administer another 50ug of my blotter now totaling at 100ug. And go back outside to the fire and crack a beer with S, some caual conversation begins and I notice some pretty extreme time dilation and colors become rather interesting. S grabs some glowsticks to fuck around with tracers. There appeared to be some weak tracers and I was beginning to wonder if this stuff was going to take off soon or not. 


T-2:00 - 3:00 All effects previously noted are now more pronounced but nothing "magical" is happening in regards to headspace or visuals. My visual field appeared more interesting and time dilation felt rather extreme, although this could be due to the fact that we were "waiting" for something to happen. More casual conversation ensued, beers continued to crack open and the fire was glowing. Headspace became slightly difficult but was easy to manage. A bit of anxiety and worry infiltrated my thoughts. I began to think about my GF and the fights we were having lately. Along with this some uneasy body sensations crept up. Alhough this sort of thing happens co-morbidly for me when a headspace becomes uncomfortable. Im not sure which comes first the negative hedspace or body sensations. My visual field grows a little more interesting, I notice electric pinks and yellows mostly but NO OEV or CEV really develop from this. S is also feeling disappointed, as he says he feels something but its weak. 


T-3:15 S suggests we go to the bars and get around people, try and have some fun. Im not feeling social so Im trying to convince him to stay behind with me. Somehow we decide to part ways and I go to my room and take the final 50ug. Now Im on a total of 150 ug, but I feel that this is just dragging this "twighlight zone like" effect out. Just feeling caught in a limbo like state which never really takes off. 


T-3:45- 4:15 S leaves to the bar and at this point Im not really worried about and decide to occupy my time browsing the webs in my room. Headspace stays the same, visual effects still the same. 


T-5:00 - 7:00 I continue to browse the internet with no change in effect and Im getting rather bored so I just continue to increase my alcohol buzz with beer. Meanwhile S and I are texting back and forth. He reports feeling extreme time dilation and being extraordinarily social. He says hes having a very stimulating time with some distortion and morphing of objects in his peripheral but not much in regards to patterning OEVs/CEVs. He says its "ok" but nothing to write home about.


T-7:00 - 8:00 More or less baseline, at least headspace wise. Visual effects still present but weaker and less interesting. S claims hes still going but not really excited about the effects. He comes home and suggests we drop the 25c-nbome he had stashed away...he was really pushy about it but I resisted , as it was 3:00am.....finally I gave in.....but that is A WHOLE DIFFERENT STORY FOR ANOTHER TIME :D


Conclusion. Even when taking threshold amounts of LSD I feel its "magic" so to speak. LSD felt more prominent in the visual department as opposed to LSZ headspace/time dilation. Im wondering if the LSZ was actually more around 100ug because the alleged 50ug felt nearly exactly about 20-30 ug of LSD. There is no doubt a "Lysergic feel" and it was clearly a cousin of LSD and had I taken it thinking it was LSD I wouldn't have argued. I don't know if it was due to the way I staggered my doses but this stuff felt as though it just draaaaagged. It could also be due to LSZ longer duration in come up, because when I stagger LSD doses this way I feel it increase in intensity with every titration. This wasn't the case with LSZ. It just felt like it lengthened the threshold effects. I also felt as though this stuff had more of a "sedating" effect similar to psilocybin and felt rather tryptamine like to me while still maintaining a strong lysergic headspace/body buzz. LSZ sort of left a bad taste in my mouth because had I taken a low-dose of LSD, I feel I would have still felt some "magic" and there probably would have been a little more going in the visual department. If I try LSZ again I will take a whole tab at once at very least and maybe this will give me a better feel for it but Im not too sure because S took his dose in two parts and he titrated to his total 150ug much sooner than I did and did not report very interesting effects. One last thing to note is that I never get bodyload from psychedelics exceptthe occasional anxiety/overexcitement and that no exception to LSZ. Little to no body load reported from S or I.  All in all, I feel as of now that LSZ is less interesting than LSD. Thanks for reading.

<!-- POST END: id=12277441 -->

| Page | 19 |

Thanks for sharing a detailed report. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  I am willing to bet a large sum of money that your experience would have been significantly stronger and different had you taken it all at once, or taken 100ug at first and then a 50ug redose.  Tolerance to psychedelics develops very quickly, so staggering doses is a good way to make the effects substantially stronger.  I find that unless I redose substantially larger than the original dose, beyond the an short initial time period, the nature of the first dose will dominate the rest of the trip.

<!-- POST END: id=12277505 -->

I think this may be due to slower onset of LSZ...it was toooooo sloooow to be interesting.


But you are right I will try it again in the method that you mention. Have you tried Al-LAD? Do you like one more than the other?

No one knows for sure how stable it is yet. Compared to AL-LAD, I think it should in theory be a little bit more stables, so if you found the method worked fine for AL-LAD, should be fine for LSZ. Keep it in orig packaging, don't open it until you must, keep it out of any light, keep it cool, should be good.

Just got my LSZ, looking forward to my first psychedelic experience i've been wanting one for ages man. I'll be doing it in a common setting with a sitter and a few other mates. Can you can swallow it straight away and have maximum effects? or should I chew it / let it sit on my tounge for a while? Any recommended movies / shows / music I should get for the trip? Sticking to 150ug for the first time, will go up after if all goes well, or I will try to get ahold of some AL-LAD after. Hopefully the comeup anxiety isn't too much like i've experienced on MDMA.

<!-- POST START: id=12281659 num=386 author=perpetualdawn author_id=307995 date=2014-04-17T17:25:35+0100 -->
### Post #386

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12281659 |
| Author | perpetualdawn |
| Author ID | 307995 |
| Date | Apr 17, 2014 at 5:25 PM |
| Page | 20 |

You can swallow it right away, it's the recommended ROA these days, as a precaution against accidentally ingesting NBOMe. If you have the standard, mail-order LSZ blotter with LSZ printed on it, it should be fine though. I found the tabs were a bit big to go down smooth, so give it a quick chew, and down the hatch.


I recommend that you set aside some music you love beforehand so that it's ready to go, so you don't have to fuss whilst tripping. For movies, I think the sort of movies without dialogue are good, like Samsara, Manufactured Landscapes, Microcosmos etc.. although that's just a guess, I rarely want to sit down to watch a screen while tripping. 


I felt some mild anxiety during comeup of LSZ, maybe more like restlessness, nothing too much though.

<!-- POST END: id=12281659 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12299254 num=390 author=Si Dread author_id=31324 date=2014-04-25T13:05:12+0100 -->
### Post #390

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12299254 |
| Author | Si Dread |
| Author ID | 31324 |
| Date | Apr 25, 2014 at 1:05 PM |
| Page | 20 |

> [Jim0 said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12281485)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Sticking to 150ug for the first time, will go up after if all goes well, or I will try to get ahold of some AL-LAD after. Hopefully the comeup anxiety isn't too much like i've experienced on MDMA.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Jim0 said:


I have similar problems, I always get the fear on the come-up. Staggering my dose & incremental dosing seems to help. My first MDMA dose was half a caps worth, I suspect they were strong though, maybe 175mg in a whole cap. From then on my doses have dropped & I rarely use more than 100mg in 4 doses these days.


Same goes for psyches. With a drug such as LSz, the duration makes it easy to peak without having to dose 150ug in one go. If I am really nervous, I'll do a quarter, followed an hour later by another quarter, saving the last half for until I'm 100% sure I'm ready to continue. If I'm a bit more confident probably two halves, or even 3/4 of a tab followd by a half tab or the same again later if I'm really in the mood! No matter what though, I almost always stagger my doses & if I don't, I often regret it. 


Bear in mind staggering the dose will stretch out an already medium length experience, & that an adrenergic tail end sometimes prevents sleep for a further couple hours at least.

<!-- POST END: id=12299254 -->

> [Si Ingwe said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12299254)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I have similar problems, I always get the fear on the come-up. Staggering my dose & incremental dosing seems to help. My first MDMA dose was half a caps worth, I suspect they were strong though, maybe 175mg in a whole cap. From then on my doses have dropped & I rarely use more than 100mg in 4 doses these days.
> 
> 
> 
> Same goes for psyches. With a drug such as LSz, the duration makes it easy to peak without having to dose 150ug in one go. If I am really nervous, I'll do a quarter, followed an hour later by another quarter, saving the last half for until I'm 100% sure I'm ready to continue. If I'm a bit more confident probably two halves, or even 3/4 of a tab followd by a half tab or the same again later if I'm really in the mood! No matter what though, I almost always stagger my doses & if I don't, I often regret it. 
> 
> 
> 
> Bear in mind staggering the dose will stretch out an already medium length experience, & that an adrenergic tail end sometimes prevents sleep for a further couple hours at least.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Si Ingwe said:


I usually stagger mine too! Im still trying to find the perfect formula for staggering. Everytime I do it I get better at it. Mushrooms are one substance that I will always stagger....to lessen the inevitable uncomfortable peak. It always uncomfortable for me anyway. Al-lad I found to be a bit gentler on the psyche so I do see much of a need to stagger unless I dose very high

| Page | 20 |

Took a tab tonight for my first psy, pretty dissapointed man.


Took  half the tab at 5:00pm, chewed for 10 minutes and swollowed. Took the  other half 30 mins later at 5:30. Noticed a bit of nausia and anxiety an  hour later and a really uncomfortable body feeling. By half 6 / 7 I  felt like I was stoned which was pretty good apart from my body feeling  heavy as fuck. For 2 hours food tasted better, music sounded better and  was laughing alot, not much euphoria or anything though just random  laughter. Constantly had this pretty horrible pain / feeling in my  stomach and tremors which ruined it. Like stomach cramping, some muscle  pain and sickness, had some dark chocolate and it seemed to ease about  10pm ish. Saw no visuals really apart from when I moved my phone  around in the dark and didn't focus on it I could see trails of the  screen. That was cool as fuck, but still not much compared to what I  expected. My thoughts were normal for the most part too, not much deep /  different thinking or anything.


So yeah, not what expected.  Will wait for the next batch of AL-LAD I reckon. Maybe 2 tabs would've  been needed for proper visuals and trip, but i'm not sure if I could  handle the side effects from 2.

### Post #396

| Page | 20 |

Meh , dose curve response is steep....if you get a chance you may only need to take 1.5 tabs to reach a good level. Ive noticed body load is more noticeable with psychedelics at lower doses. For me anyway. I believe its several reasons. First because its a powerful mind altering substance which creates distorted awareness of you body. Partial distorted awareness can feel awkward , kind of like a state of limbo, if you will. second, if you are relating body load to feelings of queeziness and tension, psychedelics tend help you not totice at higher doses because you are focused on the good effects as opposed to the side effects. Just my opinion. I can see LSZ being more interesting at higher doses. you and I sort of dosed similarly but I staggered mine even more so I probably got even less pronounced effects but I did not find it uncomfortable in the slightest

<!-- POST END: id=12302713 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12303339 num=398 author=Si Dread author_id=31324 date=2014-04-27T11:33:19+0100 -->
### Post #398

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12303339 |
| Author | Si Dread |
| Author ID | 31324 |
| Date | Apr 27, 2014 at 11:33 AM |
| Page | 20 |

In some cases, increasing the dose increases the actual effects enough to distract the tripper from body-load etc. In *some* cases!


Psychedelics are so unpredictable anyway, I'm not going to list every reason their effects vary so wildly, but I'm sure it would suffice to say that unless you really hate it or suffer some wierd reaction, you need to try varying doses & settings for a new psyche & there's no way you can judge new material after just one whirl. 


To make my point, I can assure you that a single tab of either Al-Lad or LSz, in one go, is considerably different in effect, to the best of my experience, to a single tab ingested in two seperate havles. 


Bear in mind also that the vendor who has brought these to market knows only that they are psychedelic compounds & not what possible dangerous side effects might appear at higher doses. It may cme to pass that these new psyches are better dosed at 200ug per tab rather than 150ug, but introducing new compounds at high doses is foolhardy at the least.

<!-- POST END: id=12303339 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12335169 num=407 author=jason7 author_id=207918 date=2014-05-11T22:00:42+0100 -->
### Post #407

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12335169 |
| Author | jason7 |
| Author ID | 207918 |
| Date | May 11, 2014 at 10:00 PM |
| Page | 21 |

Hi everybody, I posted in this thread several months ago about the possibility of the herb Kudzu being able to reduce the undesirable physical effects of LSZ. At that time I was unable to get Kudzu capsules where I live so I wasn't able to test it out then but I was recently able to get some so I did do the test. I took the "Kudzu challenge", as I called it since nobody had ever combined Kudzu and LSZ before, or at least not reported doing so in any forum. 


I took 2 capsules of Kudzu root, 613 mg each, and then immediately took 150 mcg LSZ (chewed the blotter a while and swallowed). What happened was that there were hardly any unpleasant effects at all, just slight stomach discomfort. Every other time I used LSZ I had quite unpleasant nausea and agitation for the first 3 hours or so. Now, I can't say that it was actually pleasant but it was only slightly UNpleasant, which is good for LSZ. It was like a low dose of LSD without the pleasurable physical aspects or pronounced visuals thereof. To me, LSD has an almost amphetamine-like body orgasm type quality and LSZ just doesn't have that for me. On the plus side there were only slight tremors whereas LSD has rather severe tremors in may case. 


My overall impression of the LSZ/Kudzu trip is that it was something to do but I wouldn't go out of my way to repeat it like I would with LSD. There is just no pleasurable reinforcing aspect to it that would compel me to repeat. The important thing, in regard to my experiment, is that the Kudzu did seem to have a positive effect but could not actually turn LSZ into LSD. Another thing I may try sometime is Curcumin, which is also supposed to be a 5-ht2c antagonist like Kudzu, which is why I thought Kudzu might cut the nausea etc in the first place. Kudzu on its own was insufficient to turn lead into gold, but it did make it considerably less leady, if you will. Kudzu is also reported to have 5-HT2a antagonism properties so that may actually have dulled the psychedelic effects of the LSZ somewhat. It didn't neutralize them though. It was still close to what I would expect from one blotter.

<!-- POST END: id=12335169 -->

Good to see you back, & with the results of your experiment! Pity it didn't pan out, I guess LSz just isn't for you. 


Do you smoke weed, tried that for nausea? Also, 150ug is a pretty conservative dose for anyone with experience tripping. If you've tripped more than 20 or 30 times, you should be pretty comfortable dosing twice that dose. In some cases with insensitive individuals the active dose needed is higher, & lower doses produce only body-load & other difficult physical or emotional phenomena. Before you give up on LSz altogether, might be worth trying a couple higher dose trips. Don't be shy to combine anti-nauseating compounds, provided you're doing so entirely safely of course. For instance, Lemon & Ginger tea, with a fat spliff as well as your Kudzu thingies, might help in combo like that.


Then agan, *if* you can get real acid, & you prefer it, might be worth keeping any LSz yo might have until you meet someone cool who's also dead eager to try it.

<!-- POST START: id=12346170 num=414 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2014-05-16T22:10:09+0100 -->
### Post #414

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12346170 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | May 16, 2014 at 10:10 PM |
| Page | 21 |

Well, I finally tried LSZ. Myself and two friends (who we'll call G and M) went camping and each took 150 micrograms. We took our doses at 9:00PM, the blotter was held in our gums for approximately 15 minutes before being swallowed. What surprised me most was the duration of the come up. It took over two hours to really start tripping. About two and a half hours into the experience, I could tell we were peaking. Of the three of us, no one experienced any nausea or discomfort, nor was there vasoconstriction to any degree. Apart from the long and very gradual onset, we found it to be almost indistinguishable from LSD. This was M's first psychedelic experience, but G and I have done LSD dozens upon dozens of times. We both agreed that apart from onset and duration, it was almost an identical experience.


The major differences I was able to distinguish were:


***Duration:*** It took over two hours to begin feeling effects- far longer than any time that I've used LSD, whether in blotter or liquid form. Also, the peak seemed to last about 5 full hours and tapered off very gradually.


***Stimulation:*** It definitely seemed less stimulating than LSD usually is for me. Usually LSD is almost somewhat "speedy" for lack of a better word. Not in an amphetamine way, but I usually find it extremely energizing. LSZ however, was much more relaxed. I certainly would not have been able to fall asleep, but I wasn't overcome with an urge to run around like a lunatic either. So I guess I would sum it up as being neither stimulating nor sedating, but very comfortably in between.


Apart from that, it really seemed like any other LSD trip. Even the differences noted above could be written off as unique to that particular trip, as trips do vary wildly sometimes with LSD. I'll need to try it again several more times, as well as incrementally increasing dosage, to see if the noted differences continue to manifest or if any other differences become apparent. Also, I have to state that I think I find LSZ to be somewhat weaker in dosage than LSD. Either that or my LSD has always just been very strong (a possibility as I'm in California). I base this on the fact that 150 micrograms of LSZ seemed equivalent to one hit of good LSD, which I've always guessed was about 100 micrograms. But this is speculatory, as I have no way of knowing exactly what the dosage of my LSD blotter has been. 


Visually it was decent, but about in line with a trip from one good hit of LSD. Some very light patterning and everything definitely had that "LSD High Definition" look to it. The body high (or body load I suppose) seemed less intense than LSD which for some people may be nice, but I've always loved how my body feels on LSD. I'm sure more of a body high will manifest with higher dosage though.


In summary, it was great! Loved the experience, it was very *very* much like LSD. I will be trying this again soon, I'm just waiting long enough to ensure that my tolerance is back to normal.

<!-- POST END: id=12346170 -->

No, I had only bought 3 AL-LADs and I used them all up long ago. I didn't like it though.  Regarding LSZ being almost indistinguishable from acid, as some people have commented, I didn't find that. I found that it had really weak visuals that were only very slightly acid-like. I could tell that I took a serotonergic substance but it was only vaguely similar to acid for me.

I edited out the quantities later, but yeah I did chuck out 7 grams of 2CE. It just had too much bodyload and I didn't even find it had good visuals. Basically it just made me feel like crap without even a decent visual payoff. Why ever torture myself with that again? I suppose I might have been able to sell it to somebody but just too much trouble really. Its only good point was the short duration. Nope, no more substituted PEAs for me, nor tryptamines. Those also cause too much nausea and other bodyload.


 Lysergamides are the only good psychs for me. Granted, they are a tryptamine of sorts, but not a crude tryptamine, a much more elaborated one which seems to make it much more refined in its effects. Why use crude compounds and get all kinds of nasty side effects when there's a much more advanced compound available? When you have steak available you don't really want to eat that soy burger anymore.


About LSZ, from what I've been reading in forums it looks like the trick to getting a good solid trip is to take fairly high doses, like 3 or more blotters. I haven't tried more than 2 since I got sick from that. I did eat some grapes right before the LSZ though, which may not have been a great idea.

As I stated a little bit ago in this thread, myself and an experienced friend suffered no ill effects and found it to be indistinguishable from LSD. My girlfriend and her friend, however, did not have nearly the same experience. She says she experienced:


*-Heavy pressure on thyroid area

*-*Cramps

**-Feverish

-Clenching jaw

-All around physically uncomfortable*​

<!-- POST START: id=12351639 num=421 author=THCified author_id=226148 date=2014-05-19T11:37:12+0100 -->
### Post #421

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12351639 |
| Author | THCified |
| Author ID | 226148 |
| Date | May 19, 2014 at 11:37 AM |
| Page | 22 |

I tried LSZ in various doses up to 450µg and never experienced unusual side-effects.


Those Pressure/Cramps you mentioned are common side-effects that Ergoloids are known to cause, which is usually and from experience with LSD/LSA/LSZ/AL-LAD, mostly dose-dependent. LSA for example, is infamous and worst in this regard! And 'feeling physically uncomfortable' is something that even Caffeine can cause, so that's absolutely nothing to blame the LSZ for.

<!-- POST END: id=12351639 -->

> Click to expand...
> — theacidtest said:


... it's very curious, but it is possible that these side effects are gender specific.


Are the girls aware that ergotomine, a chemical related to LSD, LSz & other ergoloid psychedelics, is used in childbirth & has been for centuries? If not, then their symptoms might be a correlative side-effect. If so, their symptoms might have been psychosomatic.


Equally, it could be an unexpected interraction with their birth control meds! Find out if they're on the same basic hormone pill or treatment.


> Ergotamine is an ergopeptine and part of the ergot family of alkaloids; it is structurally and biochemically closely related to ergoline. It possesses structural similarity to several neurotransmitters, and has biological activity as a vasoconstrictor.
> 
> 
> 
> It is used medicinally for treatment of acute migraine attacks (sometimes in combination with caffeine). **Medicinal usage of ergot fungus began in the 16th century to induce childbirth**, yet dosage uncertainties discouraged the use.** It has been used to prevent post-partum haemorrhage (bleeding after childbirth). It was first isolated from the ergot fungus by Arthur Stoll at Sandoz in 1918 and marketed as Gynergen in 1921.**
> 
> Click to expand...


from - [http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ergotamine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ergotamine)

<!-- POST START: id=12384078 num=439 author=Torresmo author_id=313803 date=2014-06-02T03:04:44+0100 -->
### Post #439

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12384078 |
| Author | Torresmo |
| Author ID | 313803 |
| Date | Jun 2, 2014 at 3:04 AM |
| Page | 22 |

Me and friends tried LSZ yesterday, and what a wonderful drug! We took 75µg each, and this was enough to give us a very joyful night time at the park!

It made us feel so relaxed, with a very pleasant body high. We also laughed our asses off, just like children.

Despite the relatively low dose, it exceeded expectations. 

- At this dose I, couldn't distinguish the effects from LSD (its been a long time since I took LSD for the last time, however).

- We all could eat at the peak of the effects! And we did, and the food tasted great! Thats very, very unusual for me. I have taken lots of different kinds of substances and all of them took my hunger away, but not LSZ. The same for my friends.

- The only bad effect I got was some neck/shoulder pain. However I wouldn't associate it to the drug if I hadn't read reports here in BL about the drug giving neck tension. It wasn't so bad anyway, and the pain went away as soon as I plateaued and got into a more relaxed state. So I concluded the drugs wasn't causing pains per se, but my own anxiety/tension. One other friend described a similar feeling.


Overall a very nice and gentle drug, at least in smaller dose. I don't know when but I will certainly try a bigger dosage.

IMO it`s definitely worth stocking this one up!

<!-- POST END: id=12384078 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12386645 num=440 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2014-06-03T08:13:25+0100 -->
### Post #440

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12386645 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Jun 3, 2014 at 8:13 AM |
| Page | 22 |

2nd experience with LSZ:


I took 225 micrograms along with three other people consuming the same dose. 2 of us experienced no unpleasant side effects, the other 2 had a general feeling of discomfort during the come up; this feeling subsided as the the experience peaked. The onset was very slow, much like the first time. This time it took 1 1/2 hours to feel effects, compared to 2 full hours when we each consumed 150 micrograms.


Otherwise the experience was much the same as the first. Very similar to LSD, though having done some amazing liquid LSD recently I think I can definitely tell the experiences apart. It was visual in a sort of mild acid way, certainly less visual than 225 mics of LSD would have been. The body high was definitely more strongly apparent, though less intense and less "pushy" than it is with LSD. Music appreciation was greatly enhanced, we spent a great deal of time watching a Les Claypool DVD and also were pretty blown away listening to Dark Side of The Moon.


All in all, quite pleasant and we'll definitely be pushing the dose higher next time.

<!-- POST END: id=12386645 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12388338 num=442 author=texasmedicine author_id=319236 date=2014-06-04T00:12:07+0100 -->
### Post #442

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12388338 |
| Author | texasmedicine |
| Author ID | 319236 |
| Date | Jun 4, 2014 at 12:12 AM |
| Page | 23 |

I took 150ug of this with a friend on Sunday. Swallowed tab at 11:00, took about an hour before it started to kick in. There was a bit of unpleasant body load on the come up (tremors and an upset stomach), but this smoothed out by the time the peak came around. Very pretty visuals, great enhancement of music. A typical and very enjoyable psychedelic experience. The peak was from 14:00 to 16:00. By 18:00 I was coming down quickly and was happy to travel back across the city to my home. Felt completely back to normal by 21:00.


The following day I noticed two reasonably large unexplained bruises on my legs, one just below my knee, one on my shin. Can't attribute it to the drug for sure, but can't think of another cause.


This felt very similar to LSD, just with a slightly more intense body load, unpleasant on the come up. I would be willing to dose higher, but I can easily imagine that above 300ug or so the uncomfortable body load would outweigh the positives.

<!-- POST END: id=12388338 -->

My next experience with this will definitely be at least 300ug. I honestly found 225ug to be somewhat underwhelming, I expected it to be a much greater increase in intensity compared to 150ug. I figure I'll keep pushing the dose higher until the body load becomes unpleasant. I'm also thinking that the next time I dip into my liquid LSD, I'll be trying 1 hit of LSD combined with 150ug of LSZ. A friend of mine tried this about a week ago and said it was excellent and that the duration of the two combined was much greater than either alone.

<!-- POST START: id=12388419 num=444 author=professseur author_id=317448 date=2014-06-04T00:59:43+0100 -->
### Post #444

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12388419 |
| Author | professseur |
| Author ID | 317448 |
| Date | Jun 4, 2014 at 12:59 AM |
| Page | 23 |

I had a 150ug experience the other day for the first time with LSZ, or  any lsergamide (sp?). It took about an hour to notice any changes and  slowly rose to a peak at 2.5-3 hours from ingestion. I found the feeling  very spiritual or personally meaningful, however you define it. I had  made a list of things for myself to ponder under the influence and upon  reading them I was very strongly emotionally inspired to overcome  personal problems and to better myself. I felt like 'myself' in a way I  hadn't for quite some time and it was very refreshing. The next morning I  went through with what i had promised myself and disposed of a sizable  stash of drugs that were causing harm in my life and relationships.


I  was having anxiety prior to the trip and once it kicked in, it  continued for a while with a fast heart beat (it was fast before  ingestion too). After I had reached an agreement with myself on my  personal issues, I felt much more calm and relaxed more, about 3-4 hours  into the trip. Around the point I put on some music (The Beatles -  White album) and the listening experience was orgasmic and amazing,  indescribable even. The trip tapered off, coming down around 6-7 hours  after ingestion, but after effects lingered several more hours and I had  trouble sleeping. The next day I was very tired, but in a fantastic  mood, which still persists until today, 4 days later.


Visuals  were relatively subtle; brightened and saturated colours, a mild 'fish  eye' type distortion, some movement in my peripheral vision. The closed  eye visuals I think were more impressive, but I have a hard time  remembering. I also had some muscle tension, mostly pronounced in the  first 4 hours, though it was not uncomfortable. Compared to 2c-e, maybe  1/3rd as much tension.


All in all an absolutely fantastic psychedelic. It felt a lot more powerful than I was expecting from one hit!

<!-- POST END: id=12388419 -->

> [doppelgänger said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12390732)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Is LSZ more potent than AL-LAD (in vivo)?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — doppelgänger said:


The (S,S)-(+) isomer (which is what is supposedly being sold) should be in theory the most potent one so far (even more than LSD). Irl I'd say all three are about the same potency, but since the effects aren't identical (AL-LAD is more visual), some would call it more potent.


>My next experience with this will definitely be at least 300ug

300ug is an excellent choice, should be more visual at that dose too.


>What color does LSZ show when performing an ehrlich test? 

LSZ, LSD, AL-LAD and all the other lysergamides should produce the same result. Or to be more exact, ehrlich's test tests for the presence of an indole, so anything containing that should give the same results.

pic related, indole:


![160px-Indole_2D_numbered.svg.png](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2Fe%2Fef%2FIndole_2D_numbered.svg%2F160px-Indole_2D_numbered.svg.png&hash=4845de7786735df7219232b9081c5078)

> — black53 said:


I found LSD, AL-LAD and LSZ all to be unique enough to be their own things and worthy on their own merits rather than as replacements of each other, but I found LSZ slightly closer in effects to LSD itself, though I only took AL-LAD and LSZ once each, and had a little tolerance when I tried LSZ at 150ug, so it wasn't as strong as it would normally have been at that dosage. Felt similar to maybe 70ug-ish LSD with no tolerance.


That said though, of the lot I found LSD the best "all-rounder" of the three, AL-LAD was slightly more giggly and recreational and silly, and LSZ was a little more serious, introverted, and thoughtful. As I said, all have their own merits ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST START: id=12420568 num=464 author=rosey91 author_id=328315 date=2014-06-18T01:23:01+0100 -->
### Post #464

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12420568 |
| Author | rosey91 |
| Author ID | 328315 |
| Date | Jun 18, 2014 at 1:23 AM |
| Page | 24 |

**lsz trip report**


Ok guys this is my first post and first trip report so be gentle..


Gender: Male 

Weight: 13 stone

Pervious experience: cannabis, lsd, mdpv, synthetic cannabinoids, MDMA, cocaine, 25i-nboh


Setting

Spontaneous camping trip up mountain range close by in Northern Ireland. Me and boyfriend only. Day started with hour drive down to park car near a trail. 


Headed up trail and hiked uphill for 3-4 hours stopping for lunch. Arrived about 3:30pm at pre-determined wild camp site to find we have it to ourselves. 


Previously boyfriend had agreed to take it with me but decided not to last minute and instead would be my sitter. Were exhausted from the walk but decided to take on empty stomach for best results. 


T+00:00 (3:45pm)Took 1 and 1/2 tabs of 150ug strength for a total dose of ~225ug. I'd taken ~500ug og 25i-nboh 4 days previously and was worried about cross tolerance. 


T+00:20 swallow tabs bit feeling no first alerts yet.


T+00:30 feel nauseous and like my blood sugar is really low and I'm going to faint. Start to think hiking for 3-4 hours then dropping this on an empty stomach may have been a bad idea.


I spend the next 1 hour 30 minutes huddled in a ball complaining I'm feeling very nauseous, light headed and motion sick.


T+2:00 nausea begins to pass and I come out of my cocoon to face the world and it's like I'm opening my eyes for the first time. Colours are vibrant and everything is breathing.


From this point on I have absolutley no body load or nausea or discomfort of any kind. Neck is ever so slightly stiff but not in any way uncomfortable.


T+2:30 brought my Bose sound link mini speaker with me and put on the gorillaz, plastic beach album. We are camped looking up at a valley and the grass all along it was swaying to the music and pulsing in time. It was beautiful and I kept remarking how nice nature was.


T+3:30 still outside and enjoying listening to music and talking to my boyfriend who is doing a good job of picking music and keeping the conversation interesting.


T+4:00 decide to smoke a few hits of cannabis from a small glass pipe I'd brought as it had previously mixed well with acid for me. 


T+4:30 cannabis has made the experience slightly cloudier and get lost mid sentence in thoughts that I couldn't recover. Decided it was best not to fret over the lost thoughts and get down so just kept it moving on when this happened.


Visuals were intensified with the weed. I could now see spiraling patterns within  everything I looked at. The mountains were still swaying and breathing but now also rotating like a kaleidoscope.


T+5:00 was getting late and we'd been camping all day and boyfriend wanted to go to bed. We retired indoors but it was still light outside as sunset was after 10pm and it was before 9pm. I decided to sit outside alone and smoke more weed over the course of the next half hour and be alone with my thoughts.


T+5:30 visuals shifted to an intricate pattern of interlocking L shaped blocks and these blocks were rotating to cause the spiral patterns described earlier. I felt I'd understood the visuals more and was being let in on the secret behind how the whole drug was working to produce its hallucinations. 


There also appeared to be a transparent grid across every surface that had black nodes or markers positioned along it. 


T+6:00 was getting darker now and my boyfriend was snoring loudly inside the tent which freaked me out so I made my way inside. 


T+6:10 couldn't sleep and was still tripping fairly hard so browsed my phone to see what I had. Had a copy of american beauty in HD which I watched, visual quality of movie appeared terrible on my nexus 5's screen although usually looks terrific. Enjoyable watch nonetheless.


T+8:00 have snack of sesame rolls with tuna and seed snack bars ensuring I drink plenty of water. 


Smoke more weed before putting head down and sleep with no problems. 


Conclusion

Overall experience was comparable to acid I've had although I've only ever taken low doses of acid so don't know how it compares to higher doses but had a good time and after the initial discomfort which I put down to the stupid decision to dose after exhausting hiking for 3-4 hours. 


Also I may have had cross tolerance with 25i-nboh which if is anything like the nbome tolerance I've read about then could definitely have played a factor.


Further study 

Have 3 1/2 tabs left so plan to take 1 and a half next time with at least a weeks gap and prefferably two and then the same gap before trying 2 tabs (300ug).

<!-- POST END: id=12420568 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12437721 num=465 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2014-06-26T08:47:40+0100 -->
### Post #465

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12437721 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Jun 26, 2014 at 8:47 AM |
| Page | 24 |

I have a couple new things to contribute here.


After taking (on different occasions) 150ug LSZ, 1 drop (unknown quantity) of LSD with 150ug LSZ, and 225ug LSZ, my good friend G decided to take 3 1/2 hits (525ug) of LSZ. He normally tolerates psychedelics quite well (particularly LSD) and was curious as to what a high dose of LSZ would be like. He reported that the come up was much quicker than with all previous trials with LSZ. Nausea increased steadily until he was forced to throw up right before the peak of the experience. He reported that this vomiting was incredibly intense, sort of a "purge" type feeling/activity. The trip itself was intense but not as much as expected. He said it was about on par with 2-3 hits of decent LSD but with less of a visual component. 7 hours after ingestion he was surprisingly clear headed but still suffering from mild stomach discomfort.


Yesterday my friend M ingested two hits (300ug) of LSZ by himself. His trip was spent listening to Pink Floyd and Jimi Hendrix. He described it as his most intense psychedelic experience yet, his previous experiences being: 150ug LSZ, 225ug LSZ, and one drop (unknown quantity) of LSD. He said that it was less visual than LSD, but the physical and mental intensity was incredibly strong. His most profound experience during this trip was extreme time dilation, to the point of observing reality in "slow motion". He reported that there were multiple instances where he was left questioning his sanity, this reality, divinity, and the nature of the universe. While less "recreational" than his previous experiences, he said it was by far his most rewarding experience yet. He said that, for him at least, 300ug LSZ might be the "sweet spot" dose.

<!-- POST END: id=12437721 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12448063 num=466 author=David the Chansey author_id=251987 date=2014-07-01T12:19:49+0100 -->
### Post #466

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12448063 |
| Author | David the Chansey |
| Author ID | 251987 |
| Date | Jul 1, 2014 at 12:19 PM |
| Page | 24 |

I don't think I ever reported back my experience, so here it is, later rather than never.


My friend D and I took 2.5 tabs (~375mcg) of LSZ each. It took a while to come up, about 2 hours before we started having interesting visuals. I smoked 5f-akb-48 during the trip, which considerably boosted the intensity of the visuals. It also prevented any come up poo, which I usually get when taking drugs. I got some vasoconstriction, which I wouldn't say was severe, but was unsettling at times. I think the cannabinoid helped alleviate it a little.


The visuals were not as strong as what I expected from this dose, but I feel the experience could have been affected by me eating food during the come up, despite having had breakfast just 2 hours before. My short term memory was appalling, so much so that I couldn't form a sentence that structurally made sense, because I'd forget everything that I'd just said. I think smoking made this even more pronounced, seeing as 5f-akb makes me feel stupified just by itself. I felt more aware of things that normally I would not waste time processing consciously - simple things, like noticing a plug socket and then having an in depth chain of thought about plugs.


Being in public was uncomfortable for me, and it was very obvious that I was tripping. There was a moment when I was walking the D back to the bus station and a police van drove past us and just stopped some short distance down the road, all as we were waiting to cross a busy road. My heart has never pounded so fast! I've never been arrested before and it's something I'm very paranoid about whenever I'm in public when I'm high.


So my final thought on this experience is that it was very similar to my experience on LSD in terms of altered consciousness, but the visuals were not as crazy as I would've hoped for. I've had stronger visuals from 2mg 25B-NBOMe. I'm deffo gonna try AL-LAD next, it seems to have a stronger visual component to the trip.

<!-- POST END: id=12448063 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12471416 num=474 author=getinnocuous author_id=128264 date=2014-07-13T15:44:34+0100 -->
### Post #474

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12471416 |
| Author | getinnocuous |
| Author ID | 128264 |
| Date | Jul 13, 2014 at 3:44 PM |
| Page | 24 |

**Last Night**


My two cents on LSZ.


Took it for the first time last night (around 225 ug - 1.5 tabs). Drop both at around 20:00. Took about 2 hours for a noticeable effect. I dropped after a large meal 1 hour prior so that might have slowed things down a little. 


From around 22:00 to 02:00 the effects slowly increased. They're were some open eye visuals, enhance vision, some morphing and distortion (albeit a lot milder than I was expecting). Music sounded good, nice body feeling, i found myself looking up more info on the psychedelic - was pretty engrossed. I was able to function pretty well during this time. Once it got to a certain stage it didn't feel like the effects would increase. 


I turned in around 02:30. Turned the lights off leaving only the light through my window, effects were still there (again mild), fuzziness, some minor tracers.


Overall I would say this is a nice chemical, a definate LSD like feeling. I didn't notice any problems with the come up. I was a little underwhelmed with the visuals if I'm honest- I was looking for a bit more - but I will be trying this again at 300 ug and see where I can get with it.

<!-- POST END: id=12471416 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12498751 num=488 author=weirdling author_id=313502 date=2014-07-28T12:11:47+0100 -->
### Post #488

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12498751 |
| Author | weirdling |
| Author ID | 313502 |
| Date | Jul 28, 2014 at 12:11 PM |
| Page | 25 |

> [Doldrugs said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12494006)
> 
> 
> 
> 			How safe is LSZ compared to LSD? Is there any evidence of it (or AL-LAD) being less safe in any way?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Doldrugs said:


LSZ seems to have the highest incidence of reports of body load. It also seems like the response to the drug is very varied, individually.


You probably don't want to jump in at a high dose. Start with 150mcg and take it from there.


As for AL-LAD, it seems to have a more LSD-like side effects profile, in that it's exceptionally well tolerated. A high-dose may be taxing, psychologically, but you should be fine body load-wise.

<!-- POST END: id=12498751 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12501668 num=494 author=Mudshark author_id=306197 date=2014-07-30T00:25:06+0100 -->
### Post #494

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12501668 |
| Author | Mudshark |
| Author ID | 306197 |
| Date | Jul 30, 2014 at 12:25 AM |
| Page | 25 |

[www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/pdf/lysergamide.emetics.pdf](http://www.erowid.org/archive/rhodium/pdf/lysergamide.emetics.pdf)


9,10 dihydrolysergamides  [ e.g , LSZ , etc ] are known to have emetic activity [ or as tested in canines anyway in the above reference ] . 


Unfortunately there is no human experimental data reports  [ that I can locate ] , however , I suspect that the above referenced report may help explain the " body load " and nausea of LSZ , etc .

<!-- POST END: id=12501668 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12502064 num=495 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2014-07-30T04:20:29+0100 -->
### Post #495

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12502064 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Jul 30, 2014 at 4:20 AM |
| Page | 25 |

I dosed 300ug of LSZ yesterday. It was fun and relaxing, with no negative bodyload, but it also wasn't as intense as I was hoping. It seems to me that LSZ can only really take you so far. It was enjoyable, but not earth shattering like 2 or more decent hits of LSD would be.


I'm finding LSZ to be perfect for a mellow trip, one where I'm still capable of operating my dvd player and carrying on a conversation with my tripping buddy. It's probably the perfect level of tripping for most people, but I'll definitely be keeping some actual LSD around for when I really want to go all out.


For other times though, LSZ is quite nice. At 300ug I had a wonderful body high, enhanced colors, very light patterning with my eyes open, and excellent music enhancement.

<!-- POST END: id=12502064 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=12513291 num=502 author=jason7 author_id=207918 date=2014-08-04T23:54:10+0100 -->
### Post #502

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12513291 |
| Author | jason7 |
| Author ID | 207918 |
| Date | Aug 4, 2014 at 11:54 PM |
| Page | 26 |

To me LSZ is like a very light acid trip with more stomach discomfort. It's not bad aside from the stomach discomfort, if you just want a light stimulation with some minor visual effects. 3 hits didn't do much more for me than 2, but did cause more stomach discomfort so I would recommend sticking with 2. Even with 3 the stomach discomfort wasn't severe but enough to be unpleasant. 2 seems to be the sweet spot for LSZ in my experience. It also helps to reduce stomach discomfort if you chew it and keep it in your mouth for 20 minutes before swallowing so most of it absorbs through your mouth and doesn't reach your stomach. I got pretty bad nausea when I just swallowed it right away.

<!-- POST END: id=12513291 -->

> [jason7 said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12513291)
> 
> 
> 
> 			To me LSZ is like a very light acid trip with more stomach discomfort. It's not bad aside from the stomach discomfort, if you just want a light stimulation with some minor visual effects. 3 hits didn't do much more for me than 2, but did cause more stomach discomfort so I would recommend sticking with 2. Even with 3 the stomach discomfort wasn't severe but enough to be unpleasant. 1 doesn't really do much at all. 2 seems to be the sweet spot for LSZ in my experience. It also helps to reduce stomach discomfort if you chew it and keep it in your mouth for 20 minutes before swallowing so most of it absorbs through your mouth and doesn't reach your stomach. I got pretty bad nausea when I just swallowed it right away.

### Post #504

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |

| Page | 26 |

I've found (and my group of "test subjects" seem to agree) that two blotters (300ug) seems to be the sweet spot dose with LSZ. I don't feel that pushing it any higher will add much other than bodyload. 


300ug is quite comfortable for me, but somehow I just had the feeling that anymore would result in some degree of nausea. My friend who took 3 1/2 (525ug) stated that the effects of that dose were quite similar to 2, except for the addition of horrid nausea. 


I look forward to doing this quite a bit more, though I'm not sure when. Right now I'm a little preoccupied with AL-LAD, as I just recently acquired it and have only tried it once.

<!-- POST END: id=12548624 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12548999 num=505 author=psood0nym author_id=74967 date=2014-08-24T02:27:22+0100 -->
### Post #505

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12548999 |
| Author | psood0nym |
| Author ID | 74967 |
| Date | Aug 24, 2014 at 2:27 AM |
| Page | 26 |

Has anybody plugged it? I'm guessing you could get around 50 percent potency increase that way, maybe better (reportedly LSD too goes through significant first-pass metabolism). Put a couple milliliters of water in a shot glass with the blotter dumped in it, either wait awhile for the compound to diffuse or stick it in the microwave to force it to, then suck it up in a needleless syringe, stick that up your butt, and eat the soggy paper. Voila! instant increase to your return on investment. (theoretically)

<!-- POST END: id=12548999 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12550347 num=507 author=psood0nym author_id=74967 date=2014-08-25T01:45:06+0100 -->
### Post #507

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12550347 |
| Author | psood0nym |
| Author ID | 74967 |
| Date | Aug 25, 2014 at 1:45 AM |
| Page | 26 |

> [theacidtest said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12549108)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I was under the impression that LSD and its close relatives have excellent oral bioavailability, rendering plugging or insufflation pretty pointless.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — theacidtest said:

Yeah, that's the thing: the assumption of great bioavailability. But what is the actual empirical data? I'm recalling [this old post on the topic](https://www.bluelight.org/vb/threads/191798-Snorting-LSD-Merged?p=4617724#post4617724) by fastandbulbous:


> Rectal administration has an advantage (dose wise) if the drug is metabolized in the liver as it escapes 1st pass metabolism. As LSD is metabolized in the liver, it's almost certain that plugging would require a lesser dose than the oral route; by how much though, you can continue arguing about!
> 		
> Click to expand...
Others in that same thread tried LSD rectally and claim higher potency, as well.


I think the mythology of LSD getting dumped on a chemist's hands leading to tripping (transdermal administration of LSD has not been shown to be effective to my knowledge) has seeded the notion that Lucy and company can get fully into the body by nearly any means of ingress. But I'm not sure it's true. It may just be like most other compounds where up the butt administration is more potent.


The fact that LSD is usually put on media that's not conducive to alternative ROAs (one does not look at a square of paper or a sugar cube and think "I'd like to snort that or stick it up my ass") may also have bolstered the assumption that it's 100 percent bioavailable orally.

<!-- POST END: id=12550347 -->
