<!-- POST START: id=12576179 num=509 author=psood0nym author_id=74967 date=2014-09-10T04:12:49+0100 -->
### Post #509

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12576179 |
| Author | psood0nym |
| Author ID | 74967 |
| Date | Sep 10, 2014 at 4:12 AM |
| Page | 26 |

I was curious so I searched out an academic mention of LSD's oral bioavailability. 


> Comparing the findings of Papac and Foltz with findings from a study using LSD injection (Aghajanian and Bing1964) indicates that LSD is well absorbed with a bioavailability that may be around 70%.
> 		
> Click to expand...
[http://www.maps.org/research/lsd/swisslsd/IB_LSD.pdf](http://www.maps.org/research/lsd/swisslsd/IB_LSD.pdf)

If this is true (and they do state it "may be around") I find it strange that common wisdom suggests that there's no sense in taking LSD by non-oral administration, since nearly 1/3 appears to get lost (perhaps there's other more conclusive studies that have found different?). In any case, LSZ and AL-LAD may have different properties that could make other ROAs more worthwhile than with LSD.

<!-- POST END: id=12576179 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12712805 num=534 author=«§Harry§» author_id=344638 date=2014-11-26T20:51:58+0000 -->
### Post #534

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12712805 |
| Author | «§Harry§» |
| Author ID | 344638 |
| Date | Nov 26, 2014 at 8:51 PM |
| Page | 27 |

Lay low. It could be bad neighbors or shaky mail men.  Most probably the issue originates with the government. The U.S.A., AU, and others have elaborate domestic spying programs. History of mail, money orders, phone calls, web activity, ect. gets recorded. Eventually each vendor is flagged. If the government correlates your activity with flagged vendors you get flagged. These records last many years. Millions of contraband items get through the mail each year. They only peruse some of the leads. The question isn't "Do they know?".     


Nixon told us who was "the most dangerous man in America" (Timothy Leary). Americas past drug policies created the highest incarceration rate in the world. You are using the same type of drugs Leary used. Considering this information the question is "Do they care?".

<!-- POST END: id=12712805 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12751538 num=535 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2014-12-15T22:43:09+0000 -->
### Post #535

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12751538 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Dec 15, 2014 at 10:43 PM |
| Page | 27 |

Last night I took 225ug of LSZ. Having played around with this chemical numerous times at several doses, I really think 225ug is my favorite dose. Very comfortable come up, decently visual (but not too in your face about it), and a duration of about 8 or 9 hours. 


The evening was spent listening to Primus and Electric Wizard, all in all a nice and, dare I say, relaxing trip.

<!-- POST END: id=12751538 -->

I suppose it's worth mentioning as well that I've finally decided that I like LSZ better than AL-LAD. I feel that it's a more well rounded trip and a much deeper and more immersive experience. 


Don't get me wrong, I enjoy AL-LAD quite a bit. I would like to try upping the dosage with AL-LAD to 450ug, but am not sure if it would be a worthwhile usage of my limited supply. 


I'm pretty happy about the fact that 225ug LSZ puts me exactly where I want to be. If I want or need a more intense experience, I'll probably just dip into my supply of LSD.

That could be. I thought it was stupid myself when I got my order in an envelope with no return address. That's not being stealthy, it's raising a red flag. They're supposed to use various fake return addresses. A fake one is better than none. So what if it goes back to an address that turns out to be a Starbucks or something? A thieving postal worker would also be tempted to steal an envelope with no return address because he would figure out that it's something dirty and that its theft won't be reported. Anyway, try using a PO box and see if it still happens. Maybe your current address is flagged now by Customs.

### Post #549

The best way to not get caught, send' n something in the mail... 


You should, put your idem (sealed).. into an envelope or little box... seal it, address it... just like you would have any ways..


This is the important part.


PUT THAT Envelope or box, into another envelope, or box... Address it, with a return address  (made up or not) 

 and the receivers address...  Now it is safe to send it. 


Why do I know this, you may ask?


.... I worked the "Undeliverable Unit" at USPS... this works for all other carriers too UPS FED-X... et cetera


 This is how you can get caught.. it is really rear though  ....

 lets say; something you send, becomes damaged at the mail facility... this does happen but rear (via water damage, being crushed lots of things can happen).


 If a clerk cant read the address, they have to send the letter or box to the undeliverable Unit then.... Clerks, mail handlers can not open ANY mail... or you get fired!!!


Guess what.... Undeliverable Clerks can open mail; We have to figure out, how to send that package on.... or back to sender... that's there only job...


 I get to open any letter or package 

in HOPES to find a address inside... then we have to seal it up, and send it on its way....with a stamp; saying, damaged in the mail... So (don't get paranoid if you see this stamp) Ether to the sender or receiver depending on what address we find... remember it is VERY rear something gets found ???? 


SOOOO

If I do find something questionable... I have to bring it to the attention of postal inspectors and or customs... 

No real need to be paranoid just be smart about how you send something... \


By the way....

Damaged and or unclaimed packages, because of bad address do to damage etc.. are saved, and then auctioned off to the public... any thing of danger is destroyed etc...


I hope this helps...

<!-- POST START: id=12833659 num=555 author=Toltec author_id=72331 date=2015-01-23T23:40:14+0000 -->
### Post #555

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12833659 |
| Author | Toltec |
| Author ID | 72331 |
| Date | Jan 23, 2015 at 11:40 PM |
| Page | 28 |

Postal workers don't care about what's in letters or packages sent within the usa.

Letters coming from another country. The customs unit deals with overseas mail) yes, they should have a return address on them real or not.. or change it every once in a while. 


If a senders address ever become suspect... Yes, it is place on a watch list... boxes too..... Letters are really not watch as much as the bigger boxes are... Letters, there are to many of them.... to watch 100% of the time. 


Customs will save suspect packages. \

 Once or twice a week, the clerks  dump the sacks, of save mail, onto a belt... 


Then a dog would walk back and forth and find what ever that dog is trained to find... Drugs, Plants, Live Animals etc... 

The drugs they found where always, Heroin, cocaine, meth & Pot...  I have never seen LSD or small packets of RC's  ever.. 


Remember each facility near an airport receive hundreds of thousands of packages and letters every day...


 I wouldn't worry bout anything sent in a letter  that is flat...

<!-- POST END: id=12833659 -->

So sat. im considering testing 1 al lad + 1 lsz or 2 lsz. i tried 2 allad previously, it was enjoyable, too intense for a hour or two but nothing CRAZY just disphoric/uncomfortable. next time i was thinking cut 1/4th off one blotter or even half the next time i take 2 al lad and MAYBE just dont take it or stagger the 1/4-1/2  like a hour after i drop , in hopes to lessen uncomfortable feeling....anyway thats not my real question. does anyone have any experience with 1 allad + 1 lsz ? i would think they fill in the gaps each are missing and the visuals would be as strong s 2 blotts of of either ? from what i read its not like that...any thoughts ? 


what are peole meaning by bodyload, nausea, tremors ? al lad and lsd do not give me a "body load" i consider most but not all PEAs and things like 5 meo amt even AMT to have a bodyload ime. so not ever having a negative or nauseating feeling on lsd or al lad i cant imagine lsz doing that to me, so im just wondering specifically what they mean by that "terrible bodyload from lsz" ive read about, now waaaay back in HS one of my best early trips was on LSA and it was real deal, quite diff than lsd but if i could access that pure i def would anyway that gave me aching legs, like growing pains and nausea so i guess i have "bad " side effects from a lysergimide (sp)... although it was lsa.


Also i didnt get the in awe feeling and electric euphoria i get when i take lsd when i took al lad. is that feeling "awe/amazement" there with lsz or that super electric feeling euphoria like lsd has ? 


and last how would u gauge 250-300ug lsz's OR 1 lsz + 1 al lad visuals to say 100ug-130ug of lsd's visuals ? al lad was visual but in a diff way than lsd, not particularly amazing or wowing or intricate like even low dose lsd.


ps. i just want to comment on the super high doses im seeing on lsz and al lad.... im confused 1 thats just ALOT of $ taking 5-6 blotts but even more than that. are people who do this the same people that love taking insane lsd dosed like 5-10 blotters ? bc i couldnt imagine me taking more than 2 lsd blotts ever. 100-150ug lsd totally satisfies me with minimal anxiety...so is this just a case of people liking really high doses or its just not "THAT" crazy at those doses 450ug+ bc 300ug al lad was intense not ego dissolving but i couldnt imagine being MORE confused or double what i was feeling on 300ug, any thought on that too ? also when i say 1 or 2 blotts im talking about 150ug blotters. thanks ! peace

<!-- POST START: id=12869609 num=559 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2015-02-11T09:35:46+0000 -->
### Post #559

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12869609 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Feb 11, 2015 at 9:35 AM |
| Page | 28 |

I think a few pages back I posted a short summary of my experience mixing 150ug LSZ and 150ug AL-LAD. Both were taken simultaneously. The come up was awful. It was one of the worst come ups I've ever experienced. It was dysphoric and the body load was incredibly unpleasant. Normally LSZ or AL-LAD take about two hours to really kick in for me, but the combo hit fast and hard with it only taking about an hour to begin peaking.


Once the come up resolved into the peak, it was really enjoyable. All the side effects from the onset period disappeared quite rapidly. I felt the two substances complimented eachother quite well, it was a really neat experience and I really enjoyed it. I felt like there was definitely synergy between the two, it certainly seemed more unique than I anticipated from just LSZ+AL-LAD. 


I hesitate to do it again though just because of how difficult the come up was. I've taken both LSZ and AL-LAD individually in doses of up to 300ug and never experienced any negative side effects on their own. Also, normally my come ups are pretty smooth. 


In summary, it's cool and I say go for it. Just be prepared for the possibility of a difficult first hour.

<!-- POST END: id=12869609 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=12869705 num=560 author=Doldrugs author_id=325429 date=2015-02-11T11:13:52+0000 -->
### Post #560

| Field | Value |

> [MBRC said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=12869396)
> 
> 
> 
> 			ps. i just want to comment on the super high doses im seeing on lsz and al lad.... im confused 1 thats just ALOT of $ taking 5-6 blotts but even more than that. are people who do this the same people that love taking insane lsd dosed like 5-10 blotters ? bc i couldnt imagine me taking more than 2 lsd blotts ever. 100-150ug lsd totally satisfies me with minimal anxiety...so is this just a case of people liking really high doses or its just not "THAT" crazy at those doses 450ug+ bc 300ug al lad was intense not ego dissolving but i couldnt imagine being MORE confused or double what i was feeling on 300ug, any thought on that too ? also when i say 1 or 2 blotts im talking about 150ug blotters. thanks ! peace
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — MBRC said:


Part of it is likely just personal preference, some people love roller coasters for example, while others can't fathom how anyone could enjoy them. The other part is brain chemistry. Different people can react very differently to the same dose. 300 ug of AL-LAD is barely a trip for me: minimal visuals, zero confusion, almost no effects on the body. I could go to work on 2 tabs of AL-LAD. I could take the SATs. It's the same for my girlfriend, only more so. 450-600 ug (3-4 blotters) is the point it becomes worthwhile to me. On the other hand, one of my friends finds 300 ug the maximum he can handle.

<!-- POST END: id=12869705 -->

so i tried 2 lsz blotts last fri. It was ok. I can see how people can take 600ug of this ,@ 275ug i felt like i ate one decent acid blotter minus any OEVs and the electric euphoria ive only felt on lsd. Although there were fun CEVs...


Wanting something more i bumped 5-10mg 4 aco dmt and it put me right were i wanted to be. Before the bump i was tripping , nothing spectacular. after the bump i felt just like i ate a decent blotter + 1g mush.


It was wierd and hard to explain. The lsz had a light body buzz. 4 aco dmt has a specific tryptamine feel to it diff than lsz. After the small bump its like the aco dmts body buzz lasso'd the lsz's and it felt like a strong 4 aco dmt dose from only a small amount. I think ill only add 4 ho xxx's to lsz from now on as i dont wanna eat $40 of lss at one time lol. @ 275ug i def felt like i could have upped it. My friend said he wouldn't go higher and he is the one thats likes high doses, which was wierd. He kept mentioning his jaw ached and felt wired shut...he didnt seem too have  good time also he didnt do the 4 aco dmt bump which totally turned on my trip like a switch. I kept hinting he should do some but i dont think he wanted to. Last weekend i hinted he should re dose on 2cb and he bumped 10mg and was too much. So i think he thought he would be overwhelmed and the same thing would happen.


So next weekend im thinking about re testing al lad + a 4 ho xxx sometime OR 3.5g mushrooms or a 4 aco/ho xxx. Im thinking maybe a 4 aco xxx. My friend has never tried those and he has tried shrooms plenty of times. So im thinking about either 4 ho det OR 4 aco dmt if he wants something more similar to psilocyban....

### Post #571

| Author | lamanogaucha |
| Author ID | 230226 |
| Date | Feb 16, 2015 at 3:57 PM |
| Page | 29 |

The dosage difference between the salts is too small to account for Peacephrog's problem. For example, in the case of 4-HO-MET, 20mg of the freebase equals 23.34mg of the hydrochloride and 25.31mg of the fumarate; 40mg of the fumarate equals 36.87mg of the hydrochloride -- both heavy doses that can wipe out most people.

<!-- POST END: id=12880190 -->

Instead of giving millions to gas companies for fracking, they should I dunno, give millions to Ontario and Quebec to build a High Speed Train between both Windsor and Quebec City. We're backwards too here but not too much, it's the fault of the "Conservatives" who got into Majority power in 2011, since then they pass Omnibus laws and since they are in majority, there is no need to debate and Omnibus means not even the regular conservative MP (same as a House Rep.) will know what those things contain. We get to know it little by little.


In September we lose door to door mail delivery....Canada was 15 years #1 on the UN HDI Index (basically list of countries with the best quality of life according to very large math involving other indexes. Now we dropped below the US...during the Bush years the US dropped below the 10th position..while we were chilling at #3 or so. Norway has been #1 since ever Canada lost its spot, thanks to the "conservatives", really, their point seems to destroy Canada and reshape to Herr Harper's ideas. Thankfully we'll most likely kick him out comes October, we got fixed elections now, except in exceptional circumstances, like what gave them their majority to start with, because all 3 opposition parties voted a no confidence...well vote against the Prime Minister which automatically dissolves parliament and starts new elections. 2 out of 3 opposition parties were wrecked because of how much one (the NDP, centre-left with social-democrat policies) raised to Official Opposition (they get more time than others to question the majority).


I fear we'll just drop him back to Minority government, where he was for 6 years, going mad because almost everything he tried to pass (which is more repression of all kinds) was blocked by all other parties, now all hell breaks loose, even if they lose power in october, the party who wins will be then privy to the contents of these omnibus bills and I don't know how much of them they'll be able to repeal.


I want my fucking mail at home, I live in a city of 300 000 people. I'm thinking of people living in those streets with huge slopes (Canada has a lot of that) who have no car, walking to their community mailbox slipping on the ice during winters breaking their legs (lots of old people) just to get their mail. Although according to the survey results, per area they will continue delivery to the elderly according to a doctor's notice, same with handicapped people...


They haven't even told us where they will be placed yet. The city has no word in where they will be placed. Imagine having that stuff installed on your front yard and you can't do anything about it, people will throw away all the crap mail and circulars on the ground around, it's inevitable. It's gonna such shit. I can't believe a so-called industrialized country will not have mail-people. I was only assured that when I order something and that they need my signature, they will still deliver home first, which is kind of a relief, but I order a ton of stuff through the internet, what about electronics, vinyl records and the community mailbox (basically they're the same as if we lived in the middle of nowhere) happens to be really far from me, like at the farthest point possible from my address block, I'll have to burn gas for nothing just to get my stuff. Not all deliveries need signatures, when you buy something and choose delivery methods, sometimes such is not offered.


Totally unrelated but you've brought out my ranting for today considering politics. And yeah this is Canada, last psychedelic to be banned is 2C-B in 1994. They banned some cannabinoids and MDPV (both things I could care less about, bottom of the barrel stuff if you ask me, except Cesamet, that's some sweet prescription cannabinoid that works just fine orally). I think they banned Khat not long ago only to piss off the large arab community that comes from french speaking countries in northern africa, we have a lot of them in Quebec since speaking french helps a lot if living there.

I always prefer to have a tripping buddy. Normally I prefer day tripping, but some of my favorite LSZ trips have been at night indoors. I've taken LSZ all the way up to 300ug, but I really feel that 225ug is the sweet spot for me personally. 


I'm pretty bummed it's not being made anymore. I still have some left, but I would love to have been able to buy a lifetime supply. I find it to definitely be a more interesting trip than AL-LAD.

### Post #584

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13014398 |
| Author | Thomas Davie |
| Author ID | 277891 |
| Date | Apr 29, 2015 at 6:48 PM |
| Page | 30 |

Once I got off my ass and started exploring LSZ at doses larger than 75 ug, I have to say I was pretty disappointed. Tried oral and buccal dosing..


I went 75 > 150 > 225 ug. It always took ~ 2.5 hours to kick in and was extremely mild for me. It felt like 0.5g dried Cubensis or perhaps 5 mg 4-AcO-DMT.fumarate.


A bit of light sensitivity, a slight feeling of being off kilter and mild insomnia. It always felt like something was about to happen (but never did).


Not impressed


Tom

### Post #588

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13015496 |
| Author | MrHH |
| Author ID | 226811 |
| Date | Apr 30, 2015 at 6:45 AM |
| Page | 30 |

I've tried this compound at dosages exceeding 300ug per session and I found it to be extremely visual (specially OEVs) than psychological. Sex was really nice, I remember seeing fireworks in OEVs as well as other kind of deformations while I was about to orgasm (similar patterning to LSD, but different since it really lacks the "psycho" aspect).


It has a very good recreational usage, but the body load is horrible when you exceed 200ug per session (and even more necessary to fully develop a +++ for everybody in my "psychedelic group"), so I will never do it again.


For me it's another toy that should not be pushed to high dosages due to body load... It looks like a substance for "playing" or enjoying some beers outside.


With AL-LAD happened the same to me... :-( Really looking forward to try 1p-LSD.

<!-- POST END: id=13015496 -->

<!-- POST START: id=13024814 num=591 author=jupiter25 author_id=362515 date=2015-05-05T02:25:36+0100 -->
### Post #591

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13024814 |
| Author | jupiter25 |
| Author ID | 362515 |
| Date | May 5, 2015 at 2:25 AM |
| Page | 30 |

> [Darkstorn said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=11728560)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Hmm. I tried 450 micrograms of this wonderful, weird substance and wrote a lengthy detailed attempt at making sense of its effects. The forum crapped out as i was posting it though so it's gone. Auto-save had not saved it. :/
> 
> 
> 
> But i'm not too concerned because the prevailing theme of the post was the sheer ineffability of the substance. Extremely difficult, or impossible to explain with words. It was deep to the point that words were gibberish in my mind and even the term "spiritual" lost all meaning. Deep in a very literal sense. Maybe not spiritually deep on this first attempt but... It felt like the mind was unshackled and free from subjective opinion. In fact, the internal "voice" that would normally describe the things you observe to yourself was simply not there. 
> 
> 
> 
> Yet at the same time it had a very mild body load, and i was able to perform normal (and non-normal) things just fine, while at a similar dose of acid i would usually be confined to the couch. Not so this time and my activities ranged from playing guitar and lying on the floor because i felt like it. In a very, very weird way it felt like the first trip i've ever had: Not in a way that it mirrored a previous occasion but rather that all the previous occassions were moot and that it was the *new* first trip.
> 
> 
> 
> This is going to sound harsh to those who hold the opinion that only LSD could be LSD-like but... It felt like LSD with all the druggy effects taken out. And while LSD for me is often a tool to gain greater concentration upon important philosophical questions, things i would think sober as well... Not so here. It felt like a seed was implanted in my mind and grew to encompass it whole. It was a weird mix of being able to perfectly function, and at the same time hold the dual state of being in DMT land or something. Without hindrance from either upon each other. 
> 
> 
> 
> I tried to look for negatives, but there really weren't any... I did sweat a lot but it didn't bother me at the time. It was the cleanest, least drug-like substance i've ever tried. Even compared to caffeine. And to give some perspective: I have a lot of experience of LSD itself and the last time was merely a week ago at around 700 micrograms. This thing doesn't strictly *beat* LSD... But it is its own "LSD" in a way. I don't like making predictions about the future because of too many variables: But this thing will be big. Just wait and see.
> 
> 
> 
> /E: Sorry about the lack of detail. That would be contrary to the experience itself when there weren't any specific details: It felt weird and all-encompassing. I'll need to make further tests with smaller doses, and maybe with other people to give a point of reference.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Darkstorn said:


Very similar here too, very funny to read the same about the inner voice being silent, everything was present and no meaning for karma and other thing of this kind, wird.  When it kicked in, was teleport in other reality or something, creating imaginary people and had conversation with them ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)). 

Still the visual was amazing, could see the molecules and much more it was fantastic

Yeah same issue now. I had two tabs. I took one about 2 months ago and remember it being incredibly mild and not very noteworthy (150mcg per tab).


Took the other tab today around 3pm expecting the same thing and to carry on my day with a psychedelic tinge.. no such chance. This tab feels at least 3 times as strong which doesn't even make sense... its gripping me completely. I admit the first 5-6 hours were great (I didn't really experience any mental depth like I do on lsd though) but now its just gone into full on uncomfortable.. tight muscles, abdominal cramping, sweating, heartbeat weirdness. I'm certain at least some of it is in my mind but the body load is pretty brutal. I can slowly feel the effects are starting to fade so that's a relief but overall I think I'm cashing in my chips on lsz. It was a good experiment but something about it just feels a bit 'off' to me. lsd is still my holy grail.

The LSZ that was recently sold wasn't the true SS enitomer. I've made  LSZ and 75mcg the pure SS isomer felt like 100-125mcg of LSD. And it had  far less body-load, unlike the shit public LSZ. Don't let the horrible batch of LSZ ruin your opinion of it... It was not the same as real LASSAz. Animal tests will tell ya the same story as anyone who has tried properly-made LSZ. There was ZERO body load with the good stuff and it was MORE potent than LSD.

Well, as one of the few people who absolutely loved LSZ, I feel obligated to bump this thread due to the fact that I'll be taking some LSZ tomorrow evening! My stash is quite low, but I haven't tripped in almost a year and have a bit left. 


I'll be going mellow tomorrow, just 150ug and relaxing at home by myself. I'll post an update after the trip.


I still think it's a shame that LSZ never caught on more. My two best friends and I really enjoyed it. Never really encountered much body load either, certainly less than mushrooms. I find it to be the most underrated psychedelic around. Oh well, c'est la vie.

<!-- POST START: id=13574353 num=602 author=theacidtest author_id=323039 date=2016-04-21T07:06:26+0100 -->
### Post #602

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13574353 |
| Author | theacidtest |
| Author ID | 323039 |
| Date | Apr 21, 2016 at 7:06 AM |
| Page | 31 |

Well, My LSZ trip turned out great. I took my tab (150ug) at about 10pm. The come up took about 2 hours, which is what I've come to expect from LSZ. Despite having my tabs for just over 2 years, I didn't notice significant degradation. It's possible that they've lost a small amount of potency, but the experience was more or less what I remember one hit being like. 


It wasn't particularly visual. Visual activity was pretty much limited to that sort of crisp "high definition" look that everything has on lysergamides, along with some very mild patterning if I stared at the ceiling or floor.


The come up was smooth and anxiety free. The experience itself was quite relaxing, it was very much a mellow and laid back sort of experience, psychedelic enough to be worthwhile but at no point difficult or challenging. 


I watched Futurama while coming up, as I began peaking I was in extra good spirits and was laughing quite a bit at the ironic humor in the show. Once the peak truly started I switched to listening to music through headphones. Music appreciation was everything I hoped it would be. I drank a few beers slowly throughout the duration of the experience and was able to sleep about 8 hours after ingesting my tab (which would be about 6 hours into tripping). I was definitely still feeling the effects, but tired enough that sleep came without much difficulty.

<!-- POST END: id=13574353 -->

Any of you guys hear about that vendor that was selling weak lsd as lsz up until recently? Crazy stuff. Another vendor bought some and sent it in for lab testing and they said it was like 36mcg of lsd or something. The vendor not wanting to risk legal trouble got rid of it. Just goes to show you might not be in a legal gray area if a vendor is untrustworthy. Makes sense as LSD crystal seems to be quite a decent amount cheaper than these novel lysergimides, this should be noted when working with less reputable sources.

This one came with a very "stoning" come-up for me, which I didn't particularly liked, but the second half of the trip was very dreamy and introspective. It had few visuals for me. Looking back I regret doing that, it was a unique substance. I wonder why it didn't took off and faded away.

<!-- POST START: id=13986304 num=614 author=cj187 author_id=387901 date=2017-03-21T03:28:40+0000 -->
### Post #614

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 13986304 |
| Author | cj187 |
| Author ID | 387901 |
| Date | Mar 21, 2017 at 3:28 AM |
| Page | 31 |

After trying LSZ once a few years ago, I recently decided to try it  again. Last month, I took 150ug and had an enjoyable but underwhelming  experience. Today I took 225ug and had a great time.


The first  time I tried LSZ, I experienced the body load that many people complain  about, and it made me not want to try it again. But now, LSZ gives me  absolutely no discomfort. I think it's because I'm in better physical  shape now. I eat healthy and work out almost every day now. LSZ without  the body load is pretty damn fun.


LSZ is not as visual or as  magical as LSD, but it has a nice mellow dreamy high. I took a walk  downtown and constantly struggled not to burst into laughter as I walked  past random people. Everything was very amusing to me. It was a purely  positive experience. As much as I enjoyed it at 225ug, though, it still  wasn't very intense. I'll think I'll try 300ug next time. I'm not sure  if it will actually be better or not. LSZ by nature seems subtler in  effect than the other lysergamides. The first time I tried it, I redosed  and ended up taking 450ug, and the higher dose mostly just increased  the side effects.

<!-- POST END: id=13986304 -->

The same lsz sold as a rc was actually used in a scientific study published under the name 'Return of the lysergamides. Part II Analytical and behavioural characterization of N6-allyl-6-norlysergic acid diethylamide (AL-LAD) and (2S,4S)-lysergic acid 2,4-dimethylazetidide (LSZ) Return of the lysergamides' so I guess it was the SS enantiomer since it's claimed to be that one there too.

<!-- POST START: id=14503395 num=621 author=lamanogaucha author_id=230226 date=2019-03-30T02:51:47+0000 -->
### Post #621

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14503395 |
| Author | lamanogaucha |
| Author ID | 230226 |
| Date | Mar 30, 2019 at 2:51 AM |
| Page | 32 |

Here's a little report after tonight's test...


I felt a vague "something" approximately forty-five minutes after ingestion of 300ug. This ambiguous sensation didn't turn into a true onset for another thirty minutes. The onset was steady, but very sluggish and uneventful.


At two hours, I felt as if this wasn't going to go very far, so I ingested another 150ug. Fifteen minutes after that, the onset became more rapid and pronounced, but not necessarily forceful -- it was rather smooth, in fact. This onset continued for a surprising two additional hours; the peak, which arrived over four hours after the initial dose was taken, was heady and rewarding.


Curiously, visuals were not particularly prominent until past the seventh hour. At that time, and for the next two hours, visual effects -- with open and closed eyes -- were obvious, albeit not very brightly colored.


The easy return to baseline took three hours, bringing the total duration of the experience to twelve.


Worthy of note was the odd lack of humor throughout the entirely of the test. On the other hand, good things like depth, introspection, creativity, empathy, libido and aesthetic appreciation were abundantly present.


Overall, I would describe this experience as having had a serious tone, but that seems to be typical for me while under the influence of LSZ. My tests from years ago had a similar character.

<!-- POST END: id=14503395 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14503899 num=624 author=lamanogaucha author_id=230226 date=2019-03-31T07:18:23+0100 -->
### Post #624

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14503899 |
| Author | lamanogaucha |
| Author ID | 230226 |
| Date | Mar 31, 2019 at 7:18 AM |
| Page | 32 |

Hey, Star. For me, 150ug is too mild -- an underdose, which is wasteful and annoying -- but 300-450ug is fine. I prefer 450ug, but 300ug is decent enough. Since you're very experienced with psychedelics, I would recommend 375ug. With that dose, you should have a reasonably strong experience without having to worry about becoming overwhelmed. After that, you can adjust future doses up or down, if necessary.


Keep in mind that the onset tends to be unusually slow (as with 2C-P); be patient and the reward will probably come. Also, an LSZ trip's potentially somber tone means that set and setting is probably even more important than usual.

<!-- POST END: id=14503899 -->

I'd say 300ug is maybe like 100ug LSD so quite inline 225ug equalling 75ug. It's less visual, euphoric and seems to lack most of the spiritual and intellectual aspects of LSD (and yes very slow) - it's very stripped back compared with L but being less head fucky could make it potentially good for some situations. 450ug sounds like more of a dose but the side effects the times I tried 300 didn't make me very keen to go higher but it does have it's fans

<!-- POST START: id=14547530 num=626 author=white55 author_id=379876 date=2019-05-11T21:43:04+0100 -->
### Post #626

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14547530 |
| Author | white55 |
| Author ID | 379876 |
| Date | May 11, 2019 at 9:43 PM |
| Page | 32 |

Lsz is kinda meh, it's not bad but nothing special. Messing around R2/R3 (lsz, mipla, eipla, ...) destroys the magic of lysergamides imo. The diethyl amide is necessary to retain the magic. R6 subs keep the magic too, and are all unique vs lsd, but still feel like lysergamides. R1 subs retain the magic too most of the time... shorter subs like 1a or 1p lsd are better at retaining the magic but longer ones tend to lose some magic and potency (see 1b-lsd).


300 ug is a nice dose for lsz, about as intense as 150 or maybe 200 ug lsd/1a-lsd/1p-lsd, but more boring both mentally and visually. Higher doses  cause nausea to most people so increasing the dose isn't a good idea for most. If you haven't tried it, you haven't missed anything special. It was ok, but not something that I'd love to see return (I'd love more R6 subs, the few great R1 subs and combinations of R6 and R1 subs (1a-eth-lad for example)).

<!-- POST END: id=14547530 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14563911 num=629 author=The Shadow Self author_id=279177 date=2019-06-06T20:12:39+0100 -->
### Post #629

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14563911 |
| Author | The Shadow Self |

| Page | 32 |

I still have a sheet of it. I was on a buying spree when AL-LAD and LSZ came about because I figured they would not be around long. I also found LSZ to be rather odd. I do agree that smaller doses are disagreeable, overall, and that the compound shined for me at 300 to 450ug. Also, I agree that it is less visual in terms of colors/shapes/patterns, and takes a while to kick in. I remember that the best visuals, which seemed to come out of nowhere, came about 3 or 4 hours after dosing, and it all happened at once. I remember going out in the dark, with only the streetlights on, and everything just changed, almost instantly, and suddenly everything was bathed in psychedelia. And it does seem to have a sinister vibe, and not happy go lucky like an AL-LAD. I also experienced more nausea than usual, but I think that was a 450+ dose, perhaps 600ugs. It has been sealed and vaulted and to be honest, I don't know what I will do with it. I have enough "other things" that I don't go looking for it. But I am sure I will get at it again. Same with ETH-LAD. Have almost a sheet of that which I may or may not ever use. I tried it a couple of times and while interesting, the bodyload seemed too heavy, and I usually don't think much about bodyload.

<!-- POST END: id=14563911 -->

^ I also find ETH-LAD a little too heavy and too punishing. Everytime I try it I end up feeling guilty for taking a drug, which is annoying as hell. I have a friend who reported a similar effect. It says more about how deeply rooted some of our cultural biases against drugs are than about the substance itself, but for some reason ETH-LAD *really* brings that kind of shit out. That being said, a low-dose of ETH-LAD as a supplement to a larger LSD dose can be nice.

Interesting. Since then I haven't taken it in large doses but I have combined it as part of a trip with ALD-52 or AL-LAD.  Never really experienced difficulty with it though the come-up does contain more bodyload than other lysergamides I've tried.  I'm not sure why I haven't taken another full dose of it to be honest, I think it's probably about time I do.

I really liked LSZ back in the day when it first appeared. Sadly it's controlled nowadays where I live.

<!-- POST START: id=15080155 num=649 author=THE_REAL_OBLIVION author_id=67802 date=2021-01-28T11:54:21+0000 -->
### Post #649

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15080155 |
| Author | THE_REAL_OBLIVION |
| Author ID | 67802 |
| Date | Jan 28, 2021 at 11:54 AM |
| Page | 33 |

I got a couple LSZ blotters where they were as easy to get as cigarettes. That and almost all LSD analogues....but the best store of them all, which was in my country, not in europe, not asia, not USA, it was the best effing candystore for psychedelics, too bad they had to sell off all they had to european stores. Canadian customs are a bitch nowadays and not worth wasting money or even worse btc on european sources, once I got a blotter sheet in a regular envelope with a normal amount of paper in it of clonazolam seized, I gave up, after the one European source I had that never failed just closed out of the blue while I was browsing to buy, the guy was doing all the business by himself and he couldn't handle the stress anymore, making him sick physically he was saying. A shame, as much as losing that no-border-crossings source.


I never touched them though, they're sitting somewhere in a safe, in the original mylar bag they came in, they were a gift for buying something else. It never got great reviews like ETH-LAD (best happy feeling psychedelic of all time, the comedown is nowhere like the philosophical hell that can sometimes follow LSD), AL-LAD, 1P-ETH-LAD, 1P-LSD (although I'm glad it is still very accessible and that some minds out there will benefit from it, I'd rather just take real "street" LSD than this) and butyl-LSD, that last one I got more than I can spare, never done it either though, it's in powder form and well, I got it at extreme fire sale prices, I think it's one of the analogues Nick Sand invented, I think? If not, there's a butyl in there of that analogue he produced out in BC in the late 90's that other people continued to sell on the streets for a long time and still may be, once I fell in a pool with my cellphone in it about a decade ago, I lost so many contacts, golden ones, which led me to the heavy shit I always promised myself not to mess with (smoking freebase, shooting opioids).


Anyways, LSZ was said to be underwhelming in some and I vaguely remember some reports here and elsewhere that made it somehow...not too enticing, so I cautiously gave myself and my friends many ETH-LAD and AL-LAD trips. A friend of mine stopped drinking back in 2014 from a mixed AL-LAD and LSD trip and never went back. The 2015 purchased LSZ blotters are 150ug. But I would have to review all the old posts around here before I can definitely say "hell yeah, that's good news!"

<!-- POST END: id=15080155 -->

I am sitting here gambling on bitcoin going up before I pull trigger on a sample reading old trip reports. This report I assume is of 150 mic hits, took 4 and could hear each others thoughts


I couldn't tell by now if my eyes were open or closed, but I do remember looking at E, and hearing his voice within my head. This creeped me the fuck out at first, and strangely, E looked equally as spooked. I suddenly realised that I could communicate with E (or so I thought) without opening my mouth. We entered into fragmented discussions about what we were experiencing, and how this was possible.


##### LSZ - Erowid Exp - 'Lambda and The Eternals'

An Experience with LSZ. 'Lambda and The Eternals' by SilentRoller


					erowid.org
				


This shit could be epic and give you super powers lol, but unlike the guy at the start of this thread who bought a 100 never having tried it, I'm going to buy 5 and check it out. I still have the other 4 hits of my ETH-LAD sample, thank god i didn't buy a sheet of that.

I have both the LSZ and the pink 1P-LSD blotters but I haven’t tried them yet.


I had one half of these LSZ blotters lab-tested myself and the result was LSZ, as expected. 


Purity wasn’t determined though and I imagine it’s pretty hard to detect novel lysergamide stereoisomers, so it’s probably possible that my LSZ is actually trans-LSZ. I messaged the testing-facility and will probably hand in another, full LSZ tab and one of these 1P-LSD blotters. The good thing is they have referance material for 1P, so they can quantitatively analyze the contents as well.

<!-- POST START: id=15115214 num=660 author=Viraldrome author_id=503341 date=2021-03-08T06:53:34+0000 -->
### Post #660

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15115214 |
| Author | Viraldrome |
| Author ID | 503341 |
| Date | Mar 8, 2021 at 6:53 AM |
| Page | 33 |

The most important factor for me is vendors trustworthy-ness rather than the price. I saw those colored blotters on reddit glad my vendor sells the real ones. 

Back in the 80s and 90s I used to get GI issues from LSD, the problem was it wasn't consistent. One hit caused "gutrot" and the one next to it you took a month later didn't. And now it never happens no matter where i source the LSD, so I wrote it off as my teenage body chemistry not Pickard's microdots. I'm still not sold on 10 micrograms of impurities causing stomach issues, though I don't want to open the dirty/pure acid debate either.

<!-- POST END: id=15115214 -->

## Page 34


<!-- POST START: id=15126380 num=661 author=Viraldrome author_id=503341 date=2021-03-18T11:55:54+0000 -->
### Post #661

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15126380 |
| Author | Viraldrome |
| Author ID | 503341 |
| Date | Mar 18, 2021 at 11:55 AM |
| Page | 34 |

Finally took took 1.5 of these 225 mics. I have been reading these reports for so long I was half expecting Ayahusca purging or something, I had minor stomach flutters. I don't know, I got zero visuals which is a metric I use to judge how strong something is so it's hard to say if it's close to LSD strength. If I took this amount of 1cp-LSD I would have visuals, and that is much cheaper. "LSZ it's like acid but no visuals", isn't a real strong selling point. AL-LAD and ETH LAD offered something different not sure what LSZ brings to the table that is different or unique. Its okay and I enjoyed it but visuals are kind of why I am here. Maybe this shit is great for CEV's with headphones or whatever, I guess every drug has it's place. This is add a ten strip to the stash rather than buy a sheet, but if larger doses improve my opinion of this I'm open to it, next one is 300 or more. Grade C+

<!-- POST END: id=15126380 -->

<!-- POST START: id=15492633 num=672 author=Ballz_Trippington author_id=301774 date=2022-04-18T09:49:32+0100 -->
### Post #672

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15492633 |
| Author | Ballz_Trippington |
| Author ID | 301774 |
| Date | Apr 18, 2022 at 9:49 AM |
| Page | 34 |

Well...unfortunately I'd have to rate this maybe a 6/10

I tried it at 300ug

It's by far the most clear headed Lysergamide I've ever tried.... Absolutely ZERO mindfuck (that typical cosmic lsd headspace) definitely had some decent visuals but nothing spectacular.  Mostly just bubling and morphing of patterns on the ceiling.

It definitely caused a lot of neck muscle tension and some very slight gastrointestinal issues but very minor.

I'd have to say out of all the analogs I've tried this one is one of the least interesting and most expensive....but as always YMMV!!!!

For me I'd rate the analogs from personal favorite to least would be

1P-ETH-LAD > ETH-LAD > 1P-LSD > ALD-52 > AL-LAD > LSZ > 1CP-LSD

Yet to try 1V.... but I'm super eager to try that one especially!!

Oh I work out regularly....And I have to I pour molten metal for a living...extremely hard and physical difficult....but also have Eosinophilic Facciitis and so basically a very difficult to treat autoimmune inflammation disorder.

A lot of psychedelics trigger inflammation throughout my body especially Phenethylamines but certain Lysergamides are really bad.

Surprisingly,  ETH-LAD and 1P-LSD have never invoked any muscle tension or inflammation....even super pure GG LSD cause some degree of neck and back and wrist and ankle inflammation....I've been of my Ketogenic diet which is the only thing I've found besides corticosteroids and Methotrexate to help and I won't take either of those two to help...also some benzos with strong muscle relaxation properties like Diazepam really help but the Keto Diet for myself has been by for the most benefit.

My heart goes out to you and absolutely anyone suffering with an autoimmune disorder....I suffered for decades and just figured I guess I'm getting arthritis....but what is most perplexing is that I have what appears to be severe rhumatoid arthritis but my blood work always comes back Seronegative for rhumatoid factors....my sister tests positive for rheumatoid factors but is asymptomatic....my cousin has Eosinophilic Faciitis but is also Seronegative....no idea what tge fuck is going on with inflammation genetically within my family but it seems to be unusual and severe...

After prednisone and methotrexate were hardly keeping my symptoms in check....I literally watched a YouTube video about a guy who was suffering in a similar manner as myself and thought it was completely bullocks that carbohydrates might be tge problem but I was so desperate and in so much absolutely crippling pain that I just decided to try this low/no carb diet for a month and see what happens....was expecting nothing....

Within 2 weeks all my inflammation began to recede....it was probably the most shocking moment in my entire life .

I'm not sure what your autoimmune issues are but there is a solution out there somewhere....I know how discouraging it can be but if there's anything I could do to help you please send me a message I'm always happy to help anyone who needs it in any capacity.
